Et li ovraiges, quant il est en leu ou on le puet oster, si com nos avons dit, est que tu purge aucune fois le malaide de cole noire; puis le fai sainier s’il ait manifeste repletion, puis afaite le malaide .i. boin leu por faire l’ovraige; puis giete tes oncines ou chancre, et le cheve de toutes pars, et l’oste de toutes pars sens rien laissier; et laisse corre le sanc tout fuer, et espreint bien le leu a ta main ou a aucune chose, et se li decorremens de sanc te fait contraire de l’incision de l’artere ou de la voine, si le cauterize tant que li sans soit estainchiez; puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And the work, when it is in a place where it can be removed, as we have said, is that you sometimes purge the patient of black bile; then let him bleed if he has manifest fullness, then open the disease in a suitable place to perform the operation; then cut your fingernails or calluses, and the skin all over, and the bone all over without leaving anything; and let the blood flow out completely, and squeeze the site well with your hand or something, and if the bleeding from the incision of the artery or vein makes you feel faint, cauterize it until the bleeding stops; then treat it with other remedies until it heals.
de ydropisie	of dropsy
Nos avons jai dit en la division les semblances d’idropisie, et en queil maniere li assemblee de l’aigue est faite, et les signes de chescune semblance, et la cure qui est faite par medicines, et cele qui est curee par fer: si est eclites soulement; et ne doit on touchier de fer en ces .ij. semblances: c’est a savoir, tympanites et yposarche, car c’est mortelz chose; donques quant tu medicines ceste semblance de ydropisie qui est apelee «eclites» de medicines, et li cure ne profite, si regarde se li malaides est foibles, ou s’il ait autre maladie que ydropisie, si com toust et solution de ventre et semblans choses; si n’i touchier de fer, car il i a doutance; et se tu vois le malaide de fort vertut, et il n’a autre maladie que ydropisie soulement, et il n’est mie trop jones ne trop vielz, si dois ensi ovrer:	We have already discussed the appearances of dropsy, and how the accumulation of fluid is caused, and the signs of each type, and the treatment using medicine, and that which is treated with iron. Now we will discuss only briefly: and one should not use iron in these two types of dropsy: tympany and hydrops, for they are fatal conditions. So, when treating this type of dropsy called "eclites" with medicine, if the treatment doesn't help and the patient is either very weak or has other illnesses besides dropsy, such as diarrhea and similar conditions, then one should not use iron, as there is a risk of harm. But if the patient is strong and has only dropsy, and is neither too young nor too old, then one should proceed as follows:
lieve le malaide droit sus tes mains, et li ministres presse le ventre em boutant l’aigue a la plus basse partie dou pis, puis pren le spatumile espinous selonc ceste forme: Et soit trenchans de .ij. pars. a pointe, et toutevoie ne soit mie si entrans qu’il puist venir jusc’a l’intestine quant on le fiche ens, et ne le puist blecier;	Take the patient's right hand in your hands, and the minister presses the belly by pushing the water to the lowest part of the foot, then take the thorny spatulas according to this form: And it should be .ij. Parts with a point, and yet not so intruding that it can reach the intestines when it is pushed in, and it cannot bleed;
puis regarde se li ydropisie est enjanree devers les intestines: si covient que tu fendes ensus de la boude .iij. dois droit desoz sus lou poignil; et se li ydropisie est por la maladie dou foie, si soit ta fendure au senestre de la boude .iij. dois; et se c’est por la miuce, si soit a destre, et ne covient mie que li malaides gise sus la fendure que les superfluitez ne corrent a celui foible leu;	Then look to see if the hydropsy is directed towards the intestines: you should split under the armpit 3 times on the right side of the chest; and if the hydropsy is due to the disease of the liver, then your split should be on the left side of the chest 3 times; and if it's due to the disease of the lung, then it should be on the right side, and you must not let the patient lie on the split so that the fluids do not flow to that weak spot;
puis perce tout le cuir a l’estrument, et le boute, et lieve ta main a tout le spatumile entre le cuir et le syfac ausi com en escorchant a la quantiteit d’une ungle ou enqui entor; puis perce lou syfac tant que li spatumile viegne au leu vuit, et c’est li leus de l’aigue, puis le trai fuer, et i boute cest estrument de coi ci est li forme: Et est semblans a une caine d’argent subtil, et est d’arain ou d’archaut legier, et a en la partie desoz .i. petit pertus; et ou costeit d’une part, .iij. pertus; et .ij. d’autre part, et .i. d’autre; et est li chiés tailliez si com une penne, et c’est li forme de l’incision dont li escrivains taille la penne:	Then pierce the skin with the instrument, and insert it, and hold your hand on all the spatulas between the skin and the syphac as if you were skinning to the amount of a fingernail or in between; then pierce the syphac until the spatulas reach the desired location, which is where the water is, then pull it out, and insert this instrument from which the shape comes: And it is similar to a subtle silver rod, made of lightweight bronze or brass, with 1 small hole on the bottom part; and on one side, there are 3 holes; and 2 on the other, and 1 on the other; and the head is tailored like a feather, and this is the shape of the incision that scribes cut the pen:
au chief desus est li alemele, si que quant li estrumens vient a l’aigue, si dessent maintenant sus l’estrument; vuide la donques la moitiet ou la tierce part, car se tu en vuides plus qu’il ne covient en celle houre, par aventure si muert li malaides por la resolution de son esperit de l’arme, ou il chiet paumez, ou il aproche a la mort;	at the top is the handle, so that when the instrument reaches the water, it will now descend upon the instrument; empty it therefore by half or by a third part, for if you empty more than it is convenient in that hour, by chance the patient may die due to the loss of blood, or he may fall unconscious, or he may approach death;
mais en vuide selonc la quantiteit de sa vertut, et selonc ceu que les dispositions de la vertut dou malaide signifient, et ses poulz; puis trai l’estrument et retien l’aigue, et elle est retenue maintenant por le keur qui estoupe le pertus qui est sus le syfac, de coi j’ai parleit, que tu perces selonc ceste maniere; puis rencomence l’estrument l’autre jor, se tu vois le malaide soffrant ceu, et trai de l’aigue une petite quantiteit;	but empty according to the amount of its virtue, and according to what the dispositions of the virtue of the ailment indicate, and his pulses; then bring out the instrument and retain the water, and it is now retained by the plug that stops the orifice that is above the syphilis, about which I have spoken, that you pierce in this way; then bring out the instrument again the next day, if you see the patient enduring this, and bring out a small amount of water.
fai ce aucun jor, et te garde de foloier tant qu’il ni demore mais c’un poc d’aigue. Et se tu doutes sus le malaide, et tu i lais mout d’aigue, si le cure de la sepulture ou sablon chaut, et par mout sueir ou bain et au soleil, et se teigne de boivre; et le cure de medicines desiccatives tant qu’il soit sanez, et cauterize sus l’estomac et sus lou foie et sus l’esplen aprés l’estraction de l’aigue, si com j’ai dit devant.	do this any day, and keep from following until it remains but a little water. And if you doubt about the patient, and you leave a lot of water, then the cure is burial or hot sand, and by much sweating or bathing and in the sun, and by dying from drinking; and the cure is desiccative medicines until he is healed, and cauterizing on the stomach and on the liver and on the spleen after the extraction of the water, as I said before.
de l’estopement de la verge	of the stopping of the penis
Aucune fois naissent enfant qui n’ont point de pertus en la verge, ou li pertus est petis, ou il n’est mie en son leu. Si le covient tantost qu’il n’aist percier a tout .i. spatumile molt subtil selonc ceste forme: puis met ou pertus .i. clo subtil de plonc, et le lie et le tien ensi .iij. jors ou iiij. et quant il vuet faire urine, si soit ostez li clos, et faice urine, et puis li remet; et par aventure nen i couvient point, car li urine qui vient fuer ne lou laisse close.	Sometimes children are born without an opening in the penis, or the opening is small, or it is not in its place. Then one must pierce it immediately with a very fine spatumile according to this form: then put into the opening a very thin plug of lead, and tie it and leave it for three or four days, and when he wants to urinate, remove the plug and he will urinate, and then put the plug back in; and perhaps one is not needed at all, because the urine that comes out does not leave it closed.
Cil de cui li pertus est petis, si est medicinez dou clo de plonc, si com nos avons dit, si s’eslargera. Cil qui n’ont mie le pertus en lor leu sont bleciet, car aucun naissent qui ont le pertus au chief de la verge, por coi il ne puient pissier avant s’il ne lievent lor verge en haut; et ne pueent enjanrer por ceu que li matiere ne puet venir jusc’a la marris, et c’est une male maladie.	Those whose foreskin is tight, if they are treated with a clot of blood, as we have said, will loosen. Those who do not have the foreskin in its place are infected, for some are born with the foreskin at the tip of the penis, so they cannot urinate until they lift their penis upwards; and they cannot ejaculate because the material cannot reach the glans, and this is a serious illness.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que li malaides gise sovin sus son dos, puies estent le chief de la verge et le cope ausi com la taille d’une penne, si ke li pertus chiece em mileu, si com il covient; et te garde de decorrement de sanc qui i vient maintes fois, et s’il avient, si l’estainche de ceu qui estainche sanc, et cure la plaie tant qu’il soit sanez.	And the method of treatment is that the patient lies on his back, then the tip and glans of the penis are cut to the size of a feather, so that the foreskin splits in the middle, as it should be; and beware of bleeding which often occurs, and if it does, stop the blood flow with something that stops blood flow, and treat the wound until it heals.
des pustules de la verge	of pustules on the penis
Maintes fois vienent cist albathe en la verge, et est une apparance de char laide; et en i a malignes et non malignes; si covient que tu les preignes a .i. oncine subtil, et les cope et munde toutes, puis met sus coton moilliet en oignement egiptien; puis le cure d’oignement diafinicon tant qu’il soit sanez.	Many times, there are boils on the penis, and it is an ugly skin appearance; and there are both benign and malignant ones; so you must cut them to a depth of one-eighth inch, then scrape and clean all of them, then put cotton soaked in Egyptian ointment over them; then cure with thin ointment until it heals.
Et se li albathe est maligne, de pute color et depuant, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere. Quant tu l’as copeit, et se li albathe est en som la verge, et en ait partie dedens la peil et partie defuer, si covient que tu oste l’albathe qui est dedens premier; et quant il est soudez, si le cure defuer. Car quant tu le cures ensamble, si n’est mie asseurez li chiez de la verge qu’il ne soit perciez, et vient noiror et corruption en son la verge et ou coion; si covient chever tout ceu qui est noir et corrumput, puis lie sus l’emplaustre de miel et de farine qui soit fait d’escorce de poumes grenates et de veces, puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the ulcer is malignant, with a putrid color and stench, then you must apply cautery to it. When you have burned it, and if the ulcer is on the shaft of the penis, and part of it is inside the skin and part outside, then you must first remove the ulcer that is inside; and when it is healed, then cure the one outside. For when you cure them both together, then the head of the penis is not assured from being pierced, and blackness and corruption come in its shaft and in the scrotum; so you must cut away all that is black and corrupt, then apply a poultice of honey and flour made from pomegranate rinds and poppies, then cure it with other cures until it is healed.
Et se decorremens de sanc vient, si amenistre le cautere lunaire selonc ceste forme: Li cauteres si aide as .ij. dispositions ensamble: c’est asavoir, au decorrement de sanc, et a la corruption; et se li chiés de la verge est corrumpus et retrais, si covient que tu boutes ou conduit de la verge une cainne de plonc, et pisse li malaides parmi; et quant li pelz iert aerse au chief de la verge qui avient a ces qui n’ont mie esteit circoncis, ou il avient por plaie ou por aposteme, si covient donques que tu l’escorches a .i. estrument cheveit, tant que li liiens soit desliiez, et soit delivrez li chiez de la verge de toutes pars;	And if there is bleeding, then apply the lunar cautery according to this form: The cauteries have two purposes together: that is, for bleeding and for corruption; and if the head of the penis is damaged and withdrawn, then you must insert into the shaft of the penis a lead tube, and the patient should urinate through it. And when there is swelling at the head of the penis which happens to those who have not been circumcised, either due to a wound or an abscess, then you must excise it with an instrument until the ligature is released and the head of the penis is freed from all sides;
et se c’est grief chose de deviser ceu, si covient que tu l’escorches a .i. spatumile aucun poc dou chief de la verge et de la peil; puis dessevre belement entre .ij., et i met .i. subtil drapeil de lin moilliet an aigue froide, qu’il n’aerse derechief.	and if it is a painful thing to talk about, then you must excise it with a spatulum at the head of the penis and the skin; then cut quickly between two, and put there a very thin linen cloth soaked in cold water so that it does not swell again.
de la circoncision	of circumcision
Circoncision n’est mie desliemens de continuation si com les autres plaies; toutevoie quant nos faison ceste oevre de nostre volenteit, et proprement as enfans, si est mestier que nos faisiens la millor oevre, et la plus legiere a salut.	Circumcision is not dislocation of continuity like other wounds; nevertheless when we perform this act of our own will, and properly on children, it is necessary that we make the best and lightest wound for their safety.
Je dis que li ancien ne dirent mie la circoncision de lor enfans, car il n’en usent mie en lor loi, et n’en avons mais que ceu que nos avons aquis par experiment.	I say that the ancients did not circumcise their children, for they did not use it in their law, and we have only what we have acquired through experimentation.
Car j’ai veut la plus grant partie des maistres et des sainors qui faisoient circumcision entor .i. dal, et as forces, et a tout une novacule; si fuioit li keurs car il i a .ij. toiles, et par aventure si cope on celi desus et demore celle desoz.	For I have seen the greatest part of masters and surgeons who circumcised around the glans, and with force, and all over the foreskin; so the head would go out because there are two membranes, and by chance one is above and the other below.
Or la recovient coper, et est li dolor double, et a la mundification qui est dou dal n’est mie asseuree li pointe dou membre; et a la mundification de l’ungle par aventure eschaipe li fer, et corront l’uevre, et maintes fois naissent ensi qu’il n’ont mestier de mundification et je l’ai veut.	Then they bandage it, and the pain is doubled, and in the purification which is done from below, the joint of the member is not set right; and in the purification of the nail, perhaps the iron escapes, and they ruin the work, and many times they grow thus so that they do not need purification and I want it.
De la mondification qui est faite as forces a tout le liien de fil ai je troveit la bonteit de l’experiment, car les forces taillent justement ausi bien desus com desoz.	Of the purification which is done with force throughout all the thread I have found the goodness of the experiment, for the forces cut justly as well above as below.
Car quant tu presses ta main, si tailles igalment en .i. tout soul tens; mais que li filz soit bien estrois entor lou cuir; et soit li maniere dou premier ovraige si est que tu faices penser l’enfant, s’il entent, que tu ne li fais fuer que liier le fil entor la verge tant soulement, et pues le fai esjoir en toutes les manieres que tu pues;	Because when you press your hand, you cut evenly in a circle all around the tendon; but let the thread be well tied around the skin; and the manner of the first work is such that you make the child think, if he understands, that you are only tying the thread around the wand, and then let him pull it in all the ways he can.
puis le fai ester entre tes mains tout droit, et repont les forces entre tes mains ou desoz tes piez que li enfes ne les voie, ne aucun des estrumens; puis boute ta main a la verge et souffle ou keur, et la trai en haut tant que li chiés de la verge soit ens; puis la mundifie bien de l’ordure qui i est assemblee, puis lie le leu signiet d’un fil double, puis la lie desoz .i. poc a .i. autre liien; et la tien as .ij. dois par la seconde lieeure au pouchet et au doit indice, et cope entre les .ij. liiens, puis lieve le keur desus hastanment et trai le chief de la verge;	Then hold the wand between your hands straight, and pull the forces between your hands or under your feet so that the child does not see them, nor any of the instruments; then press your hand to the wand and breathe on the wound, and draw it upwards until the head of the wand is in; then purify it well of the dirt that has gathered there, then tie the wounded area with a double thread, then tie it again at another spot lower down; and hold it with one hand by the second ligature at the wrist and the index finger, and pull the chief of the wand;
puis laisse corre le sanc poc et poc, car c’est li muedres; et met poudre sus et sus la poudre .i. drapeil glueit d’un moieuf d’uef cuit destempreit d’aigue rose, confit avec oile roset boin et fres, et lou laisse sus jusc’a l’autre jor, et le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	let the blood flow a little at a time, for that is the miasma; and apply powder on top of the powder, on .i. bandage glued with an egg yolk cooked in rose water, confited with good and fresh rose oil, and leave it on until the next day, then cure it with another cure until it is healed.
Li forme des forces a la mundification si est ceste: li dui chiés soient tenves et soient trenchans, et soient li chiés ausi grant com li mainche igalment:	The form of the force for purification is as follows: the two cheeks should be thin and sharp, and the ears as big as the hands, equally:
li error de la mundification si est quant li keurs dedens fuit a l’incision; donques il covient que tu l’estendes a ton ungle, ainsois que li leus faice aposteme; et le cope igalment, et se tu ne lou pues tenir a ton ungle, si le tien as tenailles, et puis le cope.	the error of purification is when the wound within bleeds; therefore, you must stretch it with your fingernail, so that the pus makes an abscess; and the scabs likewise, and if you cannot hold it with your fingernail, then hold it with tweezers, and then cut it.
Et s’il trespassent .iij. jors, et ceu qui est desoz la verge est enflez, si le laisse tant que li apostemes chaus soit apaisiez, et l’escorche legierement; si le cope si com tu pues mues, et te garde de la partie de la verge, ce ne li nuira niant.	And if it persists for 3 days, and what is under the foreskin is swollen, then let it be until the abscesses are soothed and the scabs lightly peeled; then cut it as much as you can, and be careful of the part of the foreskin, it will not harm him in any way.
Cure donques le leu de choses soudans plaie de poudre, que nos avons dit ou traitier des poudres, et s’on cope dou keur outre mesure, et il va au desus, si ne nuira point; cure le donques, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	Therefore treat the site of sudden injuries with a poultice, as we have said in the treatise on poultices, and if it oozes pus excessively, do not wipe it away, but let it flow; then treat it as we have said until it heals.
dou retenement de l’urine	from retention of urine
Li retenue de l’urine si est d’opilation de piere, ou de sanc congeleit, ou de bowe, ou de char nee, ou de semblans choses, que nos avons dit en la division;	Retention of urine is due to a stone, or congealed blood, or a tumor, or a growth, or similar conditions, which we have discussed in the previous chapter.
et se li urine n’est desliie, et tu vois estre la retenue por la piere qui est jai ou col de la vessie, si covient que li malaides soit corbés sus ses genoulz; et li soient mis li piez sor le dos, et estende son ventre de la partie desus lou dos, et restraigne li malaides s’alainne tant com il puet; et adonques est constrains li colz de la vessie a l’expression de la piere au desus, por coi li urine est desliie e;	And if the urine is blocked, and you see that the obstruction is caused by a stone which is lodged in the neck of the bladder, then the patient should bend over his knees, and place his feet on his back, and stretch his abdomen from above the back, and constrict the area above the navel; this will force the neck of the bladder to express the stone upwards, causing the urine to flow.
et s’elle ne vient, si com nos avons dit, et li malaides sent grant dolor, si covient que tu i aministres extraction a tout l’estrument qui est apelez «siringue», de coi ci est li forme: et soit d’argent subtilz legiere chevee, si com li penne d’un oiseil; et soit li caine d’une palme de lonc et demie, et soit subtilz au chief.	and if it does not come, as we have said, and the patient feels great pain, then you must administer extraction using an instrument called a "syringe", of which this is the form: and let it be made of thin silver wire, like the feather of a bird; and let the cane be a palm and a half long, and thin at the tip.
Et li maniere de l’issue de l’urine si est que tu pren .i. fil double, et lie au chief .i. poc de laine ou de couton, et boute le chief dou fil dedens la siringue; et cope la superfluiteit de la lainne et le boute jusc’au chief de la siringue, puis oint la siringue d’oile ou de burre et d’aubin d’uef, et fai seoir le malaide sus .i. siege, et li arose la vessie et la verge d’oile moiste et d’oile d’olive et d’aigue tede;	And the way to cause the flow of urine is that you take a double thread, and tie at the tip a little ball of wool or cotton, and insert the tip of the thread into the syringe; and cut off the excess of the wool and insert it just to the tip of the syringe, then anoint the syringe with oil or butter and egg yolk, and let the patient sit on a chair, and lubricate the bladder and penis with moist oil of olive and warm water;
puis met legierement la siringue en la verge, tant qu’elle viegne a la racine de la verge, puis double la verge desus devers la boude; puis boute la siringue avant jusc’a la vessie, et la sente li malaides venir jusc’a la chose vuide, et ceu n’est mie fait selonc cest ordre fuer que por ceu que li conduis ou elle vait est tors; puis estent le fil a tout la laine poc et poc, et li urine en suit la laine, puis l’estrai fuer, et fai corre l’urine;	then gently insert the syringe into the penis, until it reaches the root of the penis, then bend the penis upwards towards the abdomen; then fill the syringe all the way to the bladder, and the patient will feel it go up to the empty place, and this is not done according to this order except that the leader where it goes is wrong; then pull out the thread with the wool, and let the urine flow along the wool, then withdraw it, and let the urine flow;
et rencomence la siringue tant que li vessie soit vuidie, et soit aligiez li malaides.	and repeat the syringe until the bladder is emptied, and let the patient be relieved.
des maladies de la vessie	of bladder diseases
Quant escorcheures ou sanc vient en la vessie, ou porriture i est assemblee, et tu i vues distiller aigues et medicines, si fai a tout l’estrument qui est apellé «clepsedre», et c’est li forme:	When burns or bleeding occurs in the bladder, or when pus gathers there, and you see water and medicine dripping out, then do this to all of the instrument which is called 'clepsydra', and this is its form:
Elle est close, et si a .iij. pertus: .ij. d’une part, et .i. d’autre, si com tu vois; et li leus chevez par coi li medicine cort soit telz qu’il estoupe bien la verge sens adition, si c’on em puisse traire la moistor, et bouter quant mestier est;	It is sealed and has 3 openings: 2 on one side and 1 on the other, as you see; and the tube through which the medicine flows must be such that it blocks the penis without any addition, so that one can draw out moisture and push in when necessary;
et quant tu vues giter tes medicines en la vessie, met le chief dou keusteur en la moistor, et trai au traiant qui est ens; si trairas la moistor au kesteur, et puis reboute fort le traiant ens; si entrera li moistors ens, et venra a la vessie maintenant, si que li malaides la sentira;	and when you see your medicines dripping into the bladder, put the tip of the syringe into the moisture, and draw as if it were a bowstring; then release the bowstring quickly, and the moisture will enter the bladder immediately, and the patient will feel it;
et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil dont on clisterize la vessie: si est ci:	and this is the shape of the subtle catheter by which one cathesizes the bladder: it is thus:
Et est d’argent ou d’archaut, et est li chiés plus haut; et desoz a .i. sein ou li liiens chiet; puis pren une vessie de mouton et i met la moistor dont tu vues clisterizer la vessie, puis la lie entre les .ij. seins forment d’un boin fil double, et chaufe .i. poc celle moistor sus le feu; puis boute le chief dou clistere en la verge, puis estrain ta main sus la vessie a tout la moistor avenanment, tant que li malaides sente que celle moistor est jai venue a la vessie;	It is made of silver or bronze, and the head is higher up; and below there are two small lips; then take a bladder of a lamb and put in it the moisture with which you intend to cathesize the bladder, then tie the bladder between the two lips formed of a good double thread, and heat the moisture over the fire; then insert the head of the catheter into the penis, then draw your hand on the bladder until all the moisture has entered comfortably, so that the patient feels that the moisture has reached the bladder;
et se tu n’as la vessie, si pren une piece de parchemin, et en fai .i. cercle, et le perce rondement entor; puis boute .i. fil fort en ces pertus, puis assemble le cercle si com on assemble .i. dal, et met dedens ceu que tu vues d’oile et de moistor et d’aigue, et le lie en l’estrument; et fai si com tu as fait de la vessie, de presser a ta main tant que li moistor veigne a la vessie.	and if you do not have a bladder, take a piece of parchment and form it into a circle, then pierce it all around; then thread a strong wire through these holes, then assemble the circle as one assembles a bowl, and put inside what you intend to use of oil and moisture and water, and tie it in the instrument; and do as you did with the bladder, pressing with your hand until the moisture reaches the bladder.
de la piere	of stones
Nos avons jai dit en la division les manieres de piere, et l’estraction ensamble medicines; et ai dit la difference entre la piere enjanree as rains, et toz les signes, et en queil piere on doit ovrer de taille; et en la vessie, et en la verge; et je le vos dirai apertement et briément.	We have already discussed in the division the methods of stone extraction along with medications; and I have described the difference between a stone lodged in the ureter, and all the signs, and on which type of stone one should operate; and in the bladder, and in the penis; and I will tell you clearly and briefly.
Je dis que li piere qui est enjanree en la vessie si avient plus sovent as enfans, et c’est signe que li aigue saut de la vessie semblans a aigue en sa subtiliteit; et i apert harene, et graite li malaides sa verge, et li pent maintes fois, et puis enroidist; et a mout de ces saut li fondemens; et est legiere li sanation des enfans jusqu’il ont .iiij. ans, et est mout grief en viellars, et est as jones moiene, a ces qui sont entre jonesce et viellece; et est li cure plus legiere de ces qui ont la piere grans, que de ces qui l’ont petite.	I say that the stone which is lodged in the bladder occurs more often in children, and it is a sign that the water flows from the bladder similar to water in its subtlety; and it appears as a vein, and the patient feels pain in his penis, and he can urinate many times, and then it swells; and many of these stones have hard cores; and the cure is easier for those who have large stones than for those with small ones.
Et quant nos venons a la cure, si couvient premier mundifier le malaide per clistere, por traire tout le fiens qui est as intestines. Car il encombre aucune fois a querir la piere.	And when we come to the treatment, it is first necessary to cleanse the patient through an enema, in order to draw out any feces which might be obstructing the intestines and preventing the stone from being passed.
Puis prenez le malaide par les piez, et lou deboutez et movez au desoz, si que li piere dessende au parfont de la vessie, et saille aucune fois dou leu haut; puis le fai seoir entre tes mains appareilliet, et ses mains soient desoz ses cuisses, si que li vessie soit toute declinans aval; puis la quier et la touche ded ens;	Then take the patient by the feet and lift him up and shake him from side to side, so that the stone descends to the bottom of the bladder, and sometimes it comes out from above; then make him sit in your lap with his hands under his thighs, so that his bladder is completely tilted downward; then examine and feel around inside him:
se tu sens la piere en l’espaice, si te haste maintenant de taillier sus la piere. Et s’elle ne chiet au touchier dou tout, si moille ton doi indice d’oile de la main senestre, se li malaides est enfes, ou ton doi moien, se li malaides est jovencelz acomplis; et le boute en son fondement, et quier la piere, et quant tu la sens a ton doi, si l’amoine au col de la vessie; puis presse sus a ton doi, et la boute au defuer lai ou tu vues taillier.	If you feel the stone in the bladder, then quickly cut into the stone. And if it does not move when touched, then wet your left index finger with oil, if the patient is adult, or your middle finger, if the patient is an adolescent; and insert it into its opening, and push against the stone, and when you feel it with your finger, draw it back to the neck of the bladder; then press on it with your finger, and push it out where you want to cut.
Et comande au ministre qu’il presse la vessie a sa main, et li comande qu’il estende a sa main destre les coions en haut, et a sa main senestre oste le cuir qui est desoz les coions en la partie ou on fait la taille; puis i boute le spatumile copant, de coi ce est li forme:	And instruct the assistant to press on the bladder with his hand, and for the patient to extend their testicles upwards with their right hand, and with their left hand pull back the skin underneath the testicles in the area where the incision is made; then insert the spatulum tightly, following its natural shape.
Et fent entre ceu qui est entre les coions et le fondement, ne mie em mileu mais au costeit de la naige senestre; et soit drois sus la piere, et tes dois soit adés ou fondement, et soit li taille dou traver si qu’ele soit large par defuer, et dedens estroite, selonc la quantiteit de la piere, ne mie trop grans;	And cut between the testicles and anus, not in the middle but along the left side; and let it be straight over the stone, and your fingers pressed against the anus, and let the incision be across, so that it is wide on the outside and narrow inside, according to the size of the stone, not too large.
par aventure la presse si li dois qui est ou fondement, qu’elle saut fuer sens travail; et saiches qu’il i a teil piere ou il a angles, et marges: si est griés a issir; et si a teil qui est souez, semblans a une glant, et reonde, dont li issue est legiere.	By chance, the pressure on the fingers at the anus may cause it to jump out without effort; and know that there is kind of stone that has angles and edges, and another that is round like a grape, from which the passage is easier.
A celi donques ou il a angles et marge, fai la taille plus grant; et s’elle ne saut, si covient que tu estraignes sus as tenailles qui sont ausi com une lime au chief, por mues estraindre la piere si qu’elle n’eschaipe; ou tu boute desoz li .i. estrument subtil corbé au chief; et se tu ne la pues engignier ensi, si eslarge .i. poc lou pertus, et se li sans decort, si l’estrainche de vitriole;	For those with angles and margins, make the incision larger; and if it won't hold, you must stretch it using pincers which are like a file at the end, to extract the stone so that it doesn't slip out; or insert a very thin instrument underneath the stone; and if you cannot grab it thus, then widen the opening a little, and if the blood flows, stop it with vitriol.
et s’il i a plus d’une piere, si boute premier la plus grant au col de la vessie, puis cope sus, puis le trai fuer, et les petites aprés s’il en i a plusors. Et s’elle est mout grans, si la covient soier, et faire plus grant plaie. Car .ij. choses avienent au malaide: ou il muert, ou li urine vient adés par lai que li leus ne puet souder; mais toutevoie t’efforce dou traire, ou dou debrisier as tenailles, tant que tu la traies par pieces;	And if there is more than one stone, insert the largest into the neck of the bladder first, then pull it up, and the smaller ones after, if there are several. And if it is very large, you must split it and make a larger incision. For two things can happen to the patient: he may die, or the urine will flow out through the wound where the urethra cannot heal; but nevertheless, try to pull it out in pieces with pincers.
et quant tu as acomplit ton oevre, si emple la plaie d’encens et d’aloe et de sanc de dragon, et l’estraint, et met par sus .i. drapeil moilliet en oile et en vin, ou en oile et en aigue rose et aigue froide, por apaisier l’aposteme chaut; puis resovine le malaide sus son col, et ne desliier lou lien jusc’au tier jor.	And when you have finished, wash the wound with incense, aloe, and dragon's blood, and tie it up, and place a damp cloth soaked in oil and wine, or oil and rosewater and cold water, to soothe the hot abscess; then re-bandage the patient over his neck, and do not loosen the bandages until the third day.
Et quant tu le desliies, si arose mout bien lou leu d’oile et d’aigue, puis le cure d’oignement dyafinicon et d’oignement basilicon, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when you loosen it, wash the area well with oil and water, then treat the wound with thin ointment and thick ointment, until it is healed.

Then raise the wound with water and vinegar and salt, and assist him in every way you know how until he is healed; and it is necessary that every hour that you treat him, that you tie his two thighs, and apply remedies on the spot.
Et se li piere est petite, et ele est ou conduit de la verge, et fichie ens, et li urine ne puet issir; si le cure de ceu que je dis ainsois, que tu lou tailles maintes fois, est on escusez de la taille per ceste cure. Je ai ja ce proveit ensi.	And if the stone is small, and it is in the passage of the penis, and fixed there, and the urine cannot pass; then he is treated in this way, that you cut him many times with this treatment, or one excuses the cutting because of this treatment. I have already proven this.Et li cure qui est plus a grant sallut, si covient le tailler au plus tost que tu puos, car il ne puet demorer, et li urine ne puet issir; et tant qu’il est taille, il est en grant dolor, mais apres qu’il est taillé, il se sent aleseer.
Pren .i. foret de fer selonc ceste forme et soit a .iij. angles fichiees en .i. tison:	And the treatment which is more beneficial to health, then one must cut it as soon as possible, for it cannot stay, and the urine cannot pass; and while it is being cut, he feels great pain, but after it is cut, he feels relief.Take a 1-inch iron rod according to this shape with 3 angles fixed in a tongs:
puis pren .i. fil et lou lie entor la verge desoz la piere, si qu’ele ne puist venir arrier en la vessie; puis boute le foret en la verge legierement, tant qu’il viegne a la piere; et torne le foret a ta main en la piere poc et poc, tant que tu puisses percier la piere d’autre part; si venra tantost li urine, puis presse ta main sus ceu qui est demorez de la piere qui est dedens la verge. Si est tantost brisie, et saut fuer avec l’urine, et est garis li malaides;	then take a thread and tie it around the shaft below the stone, so that it cannot return to the bladder; then gently push the probe into the shaft until it reaches the stone; and push the probe back into your hand in the stone little by little, until you can pierce the stone from another side; then the urine will come out at once, then press your hand on what is left of the stone that is inside the shaft. Then it is broken at once, and flies out with the urine, and the patient is healed;
et se tu ne pues ce faire por aucune chose qui le deffent, si lie .i. fil desoz la piere et .i. autre desus, puis fent la verge endroit la piere entre les .ij. liiens, puis l’estrai fuer, et deslie lou liien, et mundifie lou sanc congeleit qui est en la plaie; et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and if you cannot do this for any reason that prevents it, then tie a thread under the stone and another above it, then make an incision in the shaft between the two threads, then pull it out, and untie the thread, and clean the congealed blood that is in the wound; and treat it until it heals.
de la piere des femmes	of stones in women
Poc avient que piere soit enjanree en femmes, et s’il avient aucune fois, si est li cure grief, et est deffendut por .iij. choses: l’une est que per aventure li femme est vierge; et li seconde est c’on ne puet trover femme bien saichant qui se descuevre as mires, meismement quant elle est caste.	It sometimes happens that a stone becomes lodged in women, and if it does, the cure is difficult, and is prohibited by three things: one is that perhaps the woman is a virgin; and the second is that one cannot find a well-informed woman who reveals herself to midwives, especially when she is chaste.
Et li tierce maniere si est que par aventure on ne puet trover femme bien saichant en cest art de mains; et li quarte maniere si est que li piere de la femme si est plus em parfont que li piere de l’ome, por coi il i couvient faire plus parfonde taille, et grant paour i a.	The third way is that one cannot find a woman well-versed in this art; and the fourth way is that the stone of the woman is deeper than that of a man, so it requires a deeper incision, and there is great fear involved.
Et se necessitez semont a ceu, si covient que tu preignes une mieresse bien sachant, et a poines la trueve on, et se tu n’en trueves, point si quier .i. caste mire subtil; et li presente une baile bien saige en la vie des femmes, ou une femme qui saiche une partie de l’art, et li comande qu’ele faice ceu que tu li comandes de l’inquisicion de la piere;	And if you need to, get a female assistant who is very knowledgeable, and gently probe with it, and if you don't find anything, don't worry. Use a very thin probe; and show her a good example of a woman's anatomy, or a woman who knows some of the art, and tell her to do what you instruct from your examination of the stone;
et regarde mout bien se li femme est vierge: adonques li covient bouter son doit ou fondement et querir la piere; et s’ele la trueve, si la constraigne desoz son doit, et li recomande qu’elle boute son doit ou con la malaide, et quiere et presse sa main senestre sus la vessie forment.	and check very carefully if the woman is a virgin: then she should push her finger into her vagina and look for the stone; and if she finds it, she should hold it under her finger, and he should instruct her to push her left hand firmly against her bladder.
S’elle la trueve, si covient qu’elle la mueve de greit en greit des l’entree de la vessie jusque desoz, tant qu’elle viegne a la racine de la cuisse; puis cope sus la piere en la racine de la cuisse encontre le mileu dou con, lai ou il est mues apparilliet, et sent la piere en celle partie; et ne mueve son doi desus la piere ou desoz, et soit li taille au premier petite;	If she finds it, she should move the stone gradually from the entrance of the bladder to the root, until it reaches the root of the thigh; then press on the stone at the root of the thigh against the middle of the urethra, where it is most sensitive; and feel the stone in that part; and do not push the finger over or under the stone, and let the incision be small at first;
puis boute lou rait en la taille, se tu sens la piere si acroi la plaie tant que li piere puisse issir fuer, et saiches que maintes manieres de pieres sont: c’est a savoir, petites et grans et aspres et souez, longes et reondes, et qui ont rains. si saiches les semblances por savoir l’issue.	then pour the wine into the wound at the waist, feel the stone and see if it is sharp enough to cut through the wound so that the stone can come out; and know that there are many kinds of stones: small and large, rough and smooth, long and round, and some with horns. Know their likenesses in order to know how they will come out.
Et se li sans te vaint, si met au leu vitriole broiet, et li tien une houre tant que li sans soit estainchiez; puis revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer, et aies des estrumens que je t’ai dit en l’estraction de la piere as homes por toi aidier en ton oevre;	And if the wine does not work, then apply powdered vitriol and hold it for an hour until the bleeding stops; then return to your task and have ready the instruments that I told you about in the extraction of stones from men to help you with your work.
et se li sans te vaint, et c’est de l’artere qui est copee, si met la poudre sus le leu et l’estrain de tentes et de bendelz, et ne rencomencier plus ceu, et laisse la piere et ne la traire mie, que par aventure morroit li malaide; puis cure la plaie.	And if the bleeding does not stop and it is an artery that is cut, then apply the powder to the wound and constrict it with bandages and linen, and do not re-open the wound, and leave the stone and do not try to pull it out, for fear of killing the patient; then cure the wound.
Et quant li chalor dou sanc est apaisie, et li leus porrist, si revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer.	And when the heat of the blood has subsided and the swelling has gone down, return to your task and have the stone extracted.
de hernie carnouse	of a fleshy hernia
Ramice aquouse n’est autre chose que assemblee de moistor ou blanc syfac, qui est desoz lou keur des coions, que contient l’uef; et est apelez «syfac», et aucune fois est proprement en la toile de l’uef, si c’on cuide que ce soit .i. autre oef; et c’est li cuir dou coion entre lou blanc syfac que nos avons dit; et ceu n’avient se poc non.	A watery hernia is nothing other than an accumulation of moisture or white pus, which is located below the membrane of the testicles that contains the egg; and it is called 'pus', and sometimes it is properly in the membrane of the egg, if one believes it to be another egg; and this occurs between the white pus that we mentioned earlier.
Et li generation de cest ramice si est de foibleteit que vient as coions, et est espandue celle matiere.	And the cause of this hernia is due to weakness that affects the testicles, causing this material to accumulate and spread.
Et aucune fois si vient de percussion sus les coions, et ceste moistor si a maintes colors: ou c’est color declinans a jaunice, ou c’est sans rouge, ou noir, ou aquous blans, et ce avient plus;	And sometimes it comes from a blow to the testicles, and this moisture takes on many colors: sometimes it is yellow, sometimes red, sometimes black, sometimes watery white, and so on.
et ce sont li signe de conoistre ceste assemblee, car s’elle est ou blanc syfac que nos avons dit, si est li apostemes reons, .i. poc lonc si com li figure d’un oef, et n’apert mie li coions, car il a moistor tout entor.	and these are the signs to recognize this assembly, for if it is in the white syphon which we have mentioned, then the abscesses are open, that is, as long as the shape of an egg, and does not show the testicles, for there is moisture all around.
Et s’il a moistor en la propre toile, si est li apostemes reons avec une partie de l’uef, et por ceu pense on que c’est uns autres oef;	And if he has moisture in the scrotum, then the abscesses are open with part of an egg, and because of this they think it is another egg.
et se li moistor est entre le cuir des coions et le blanc syfac, si le sent om bien; donques quant tu vues savoir la color de la moistor, si esprueve a tout l’intromissoire quarreit, de coi li forme est ci devant.	And if the moisture is between the skin of the testicles and the white syphon, then it feels good; therefore, when you want to know the color of the moisture, you should probe throughout the entire scrotum, as the form is described above.
Selonc ceu donques qui vient aprés l’intromissoire, juge de ceu qui est dedens.	According to this then, what comes after the scrotum, judge what is inside.
Et quant nos la curons par fer, si covient que li malaides soit sainiez selonc som pooir et la repletion de son cors; puis le sovine sus son dos, sus une chose un poc haute, et met desoz lui mout de drapelz;	And when we treat it with fire, the patient should be healed according to his strength and the fullness of his body; then he lies on his back, on something slightly raised, and many layers of cloth are placed underneath him;
puis sié sus sa senestre, et comande au ministre qu’il sié a destre, et estende la verge a l’un des .ij. costelz dou keur des coions;	then he sits on his left side and instructs the attendant to sit on his right, and extends the arm to one of the two ribs near the heart;
puis pren le spatumile leit, et cope le cuir des coions parmi leu dou lonc jusque delez lou poignil, et soit ta fendure toute droite en devisant le cuir des coions jusc’a syfac blanc, et l’escorche subtilment selonc tom pooir;	then take the lit spatule and cut through the skin of the chest between the ribs, all the way to the white skin, cutting it carefully according to his strength;
puis perce lou syfac plain d’aigue a .i. large pertus, et estrai toute l’aigue, et puis met tes oncines, et estent lou syfac amont; et ne touchier le keur des coions, mais que le syfac soulement; cope tout ou par pieces meismement le costeit de lui subtil, que se tu ne le copes bien saigement, si revenra li aigue;	then pierce the plain water through the skin with a large hole, and extract all the water, then put in your fingers, and let the skin rise above; and do not touch the heart of the chest, but only the skin; cut it all around carefully, the costlet of him subtilely, if you do not cut it bleeding well, then the water will return;
et se l’uef saut fuer a ton oevre, si le ramoinne en son leu quant tu avras acomplit l’uevre dou syfac; puis assemble les .ij. leivres dou keur des coions a une costure, puis le cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and if the wound jumped out of your work, then put it back in its place when you have completed the work with the syringe; then bring together the two lips of the wound with a single stitch, and then treat it as you would other wounds, until it is healed.
Et se tu trueves l’uef corromput d’autre maladie, si covient que tu lies les vasselz que sont suspensoire, en doutant le decorrement de sanc; puis cope le coion a tout le suspensoire, et estrai l’uef, et le cure si com nos avons dit.	And if you find the wound corrupted by another disease, then you must tie off the vessels that are suspended, fearing the flow of blood; then cut into the vein at the suspension, and extract the wound, and treat it as we have said.
Et se aigue est assemblee en .ij. parties ensamble, saiches que ce sont .ij. ramices; si cope l’autre partie si com tu as fait la premiere igalment, puis essue lou sanc, et met en la plaie lainne moillie en oile roset;	And if the wound is divided into two parts, know that these are two branches; so cut into the other part just as you did the first equally, then wash out the blood and place soft lamb's wool in oil on the wound.
et met defuer autre laine moillie en vin et en oile, et met sus les .ij. coions, et met desus drapelz doublés, et le lie sus a tout le liien qui est selonc ceste forme:	and place another piece of soft lamb's wool soaked in wine and oil on the wound, and place it over both parts of the vein, and put over that double folds of cloth, and tie it all together with a ligature in this shape:
Puis pren .ij. drapelz, et les emple de laine charpie selonc ceste semblance et soient assemblez par cousture en la gorle des braies, et li uns des chiés preigne sus le fondement jusc’au dos, et li autres a la partie dou poignil; et li autre dui chief sus les .ij. angres, et soit toute assemblee li restreinture en la boucle dou braier;	Take two pieces of cloth and stuff them with wool according to this appearance, and sew them together at the crotch of the breeches, and let one of the pieces be tied around the anus up to the back, and the other at the perineum; and the other two ends on the two thighs, and tie all the rest in a knot at the loop of the breeches.
et aucune fois est medicinee ceste ramice de cautere en leu de taille de fer, et est que tu preignes .i. cautere cultellaire subtil, et cope le cuir des coions, et soit eschaufez si com nos avons dit, si que li syfac blanc que contient l’aigue est descovers;	And sometimes this ramification of cautery is used in place of an iron incision, and it is necessary to press a thin cautery knife gently against the skin, and heat it as we have said, so that the white membrane containing the water is exposed;
si pren lou cautere selonc ceste forme, et perce celui syfac as oncines, et l’escorche a cest subtil cautere chaut:	Take the cautery according to this shape, and pierce that membrane gently, and burn it with this fine hot cautery:
Et lou cope en toutes les manieres que tu pues, tant que tu esraiches tout; et garde que li feus ne touche l’uef; et saiches que ceste oevre est plus salve; et mues gardans de decorrement de sanc, et muedres que li ovraiges de taille;	And cut it in all ways that you can, until you have extracted everything; and be careful not to let the fire touch the yolk; and know that this method is much safer; and we also warn of bleeding, and of damage from cutting.
et se nulle chose te fait contraire, ou aposteme chaus ou decorremens de sanc ou autre chose, si cure ce qui te fait contraire, selonc ceu qui est devant dit.	and if nothing contradicts you, then treat the abscess, or bleeding, or anything else that contradicts you, according to what has been said before.
Et se li malaides est paourous, et ne vuet atendre cest ovraige por son horribleteit, si amenistre perforation, si com je te di, et est que quant tu es bien certains par les significations que nos avons dit que ramice aquouse est lai,	And if the patient is fearful and does not want to undergo this treatment due to its horrible nature, then administer a puncturing, as I have told you, and when you are certain through the signs that we have mentioned that the water is gone,
si fai seoir le malaide sus .i. siege leveit; puis perce l’aposteme an la partie desoz a tout le spatumile large, et met la perforation dou lonc dou cors; et soit larges li pertus, si que toute li aigue corre fuer;	let the patient sit on a high seat; then pierce the abscess at the bottom part all the way to the spleen, and insert the puncturing tool deeply into the body; and make the holes wide enough so that all the fluid can flow out;
puis met coton sus le leu, et le lie, et laisse por corre le remenant de l’aigue, puis le cure tant que li plaie soit sanee;	then put cotton on the wound, and bandage it, and leave it to drain the remaining fluid, then treat the wound until it is healed;
et se li blainche toile ne laisse issir l’aigue en la bouche de la plaie, si covient que tu i boutes une penne ou l’estrument dont on trait l’aigue des ydropiques, de coi li forme est ci devant; et eslarge .i. poc la plaie, et saiches que li aigue revient, et est assemblee aprés .vj. mois ou enqui entor, et quant elle est assemblee si com devant, et ensi passera li malaides ses jors.	and if the white membrane does not let the water out at the mouth of the wound, then you should put in it a pipe or instrument with which one treats the water in the hydrops, whose form is described above; and enlarge the wound a little, and let the water come out, and it will be gathered again after six months or so, and when it is gathered as before, then the patient will pass his days.
de l’aposteme des coions	of the abscesses of the testicles
Saiches que en la section de ceste ramice a paor em plusors dispositions, por coi il me semble que mues vaut c’on la laisse;	Know that in the dissection of this nerve there is fear in many dispositions, because of which I believe it is better to leave it untouched:
et je vos dirai l’ovraige et les semblances de l’aposteme.	and I will tell you the operation and the appearances of the abscess.
Je dis donques que maint aposteme vienent ou cors, et meismement as coions; et c’est par mout de cas.	I therefore say that many abscesses come from the body, and especially in the groin; and this is through a great variety of cases.
C’est a savoir par superfluiteit aigre et ague, qui est espandue as coions, ou de percussion;	This is due to an excess of bitterness and redness caused by a blow, which is spread in the groin, or from a punch;
et est li color de l’aposteme selonc la color dou cors; et ne trueve point de dolor, et est aposteme grief;	and the color of the abscess follows the color of the body; and it does not subside, and it is a painful and serious abscess;
et par aventure est uns apostemes griés paourous et pierous, et de fuxe color, et aucune fois vient de nout d’artere, ou d’enfleure de voine.	and sometimes there are dark green and purulent abscesses, with a bluish color, and at times they come from a burst artery, or from inflammation of the vein.
Quant c’est par nout d’artere, si est conus par la disposition d’aposteme chaut, quant tu la presses a tes dois;	When it is due to a vein, it is detected by the hot feeling of an abscess when you press it with your fingers.
et ne covient mie que tu i touches.	You must not touch it.
Cil qui est fais d’enfleure de voine est conus par sa disposition a l’expression dou touchement des dois,	Those who have swelling in their veins are detected by their appearance when pressed with the fingers,
et puet om bien faire la taille sus ceste semblance, et sus les autres chars;	and can make an incision on this appearance, and on other similar ones,
et est que tu cope lou keur des coions, puis estent l’uef en haut, et le trai fuer dou blanc syfac, et delivre lou suspensoire de toutes pars de l’uef.	and you should cut the heart of the testicles, then the yolk will rise upwards and the white part will be expelled from all sides of the egg.
Se li uef est ja sodez avec ces chars nees, si covient donques que tu traies l’uef, et lou cope;	If the eggs are already cooked with these new eggs, then you must break the egg and cut it.
et s’il est aers au syfac, ou en ceu qui est dedens les vasselz, si covient que tu delivre toute celle tenve, et la cope reondement.	And if there is air in the yolk, or in what is inside the vessels, then you must release all that tension and cut it smoothly.
Et se li naissance de la char est ou leu derrier, si covient que tu la copes toute, et estrai l’uef, si com nous avons dit.	And if the origin of the yolk is at the back, then you must cut it completely and extract the yolk, as we have said.
Et quant tes ovraiges est acomplis, si emple la plaie de laine moillie en oile roset et en vin, puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when your work is done, employ the wound with moist wool in rose oil and wine, then treat it with other treatments until it is healed.
de l’aposteme des coions	of the testicle abscess
Cis est uns apostemes envoloupez d’un envoloupement semblant a .i. borjon, avec le mollifiement des coions,	This is an abscess wrapped in a wrapper similar to a .i. bud, with the softening of the testicles,
et se muet li malaides griement quant il vait;	and the patient feels great pain when he walks;
et li cure de ceste maladie si est bien pres ausi paourouse com ceste ci devant,	and the treatment for this illness is just as fearful as the one before.
et toutevoie nos vos dirons l’ovraige de li, selonc ceu que li ancien firent.	And yet we will tell you about its cure according to what the ancients did.
Il covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide sus .i. siege aleveit, puis li boute le suspensoire des coions aval a tes dois,	You must have the patient sit on an elevated seat, then tie the suspension band around his testicles with your hands,
a tout le vasseil qui sont prochien a la verge, et les teigne li maistres, et les estende forment;	and tightly twist all the veins that are near the penis, and hold them firmly, and stretch them firmly;
puis cope au spatumile trenchant large dou traver endroit les vasselz, tant qu’il soient descovert,	then cut with a spatula broadly through the vessels, so that they are exposed.
et puis escorche de chescune part, si com nos avons dit en l’estraction des arteres qui sont en temples;	and then scrape from each side, as we have said in the extraction of the arteries which are in the temples;
puis i fiche une aguille ou il ait .i. fil double, et le lie au premier leu ou li vis est venue, et le lie derechief a l’autre chief;	then he inserts a needle where there is .a. double thread, and ties it at the first place where the screw came in, and ties it again at the other end;
puis les cope em mileu droitement, selonc la longesce dou cors, et en trai les moistors corrumpues;	then he cuts them evenly in the middle, according to the length of the body, and draws out the corrupted moisture;
puis cure la plaie si com les autres ou on enjanre bowe, si que aucun vassel chiecent que norrissent l’un des coions;	then treat the wound as with the others or with a bandage, so that no blood vessels are cut that nourish one of the testicles;
car par ceu n’i vient point de mal, et se a toz les vasselz vient vis, si covient traire les coions a tout les vasselz;	for through this there is no harm, and if blood vessels come from all sides, then the testicles should be drawn away from all the vessels;
si que li oes ne perde son norrissement por l’incision des vasselz, et sechent et ne se puient aidier.	so that the testicle does not lose its nourishment through cutting the vessels, and dry up and cannot be helped.
de la routure dou syfac	of the rot of the scrotum
Li avenemens de ceste ramice si est par la section que vient ou syfac, ou l’estension sus le ventre en la partie des angres, por coi li intestine dessendent de celle routure a l’un des coions;	The causes of this disease are through the cut that comes from syphilis, or the swelling on the belly in the part of the intestines, which cause the intestines to descend from that opening to one of the testicles.
et ceste routure est ou dou syfac, ou de l’estension de li, et vienent ces .ij. manieres de mout de causes: ou de percussion, ou de saut, ou de braire, ou de levement de grief faix, et par semblans choses;	and this opening is from syphilis or the swelling of it, and these two ways of the flow come from many causes: from a blow, or jumping, or straining, or lifting a heavy load, and by similar things.
et li signes quant c’est de l’estension dou syfac, si est qu’il avient poc et poc, en lonc tens, et ne vient mie soudainnement;	And the signs that it is from the swelling of syphilis are that it happens slowly over a long time, and does not come suddenly.
et est li apostemes igalz jusque vers le parfont, por ceu que li syfac apresse l’intestine.	and the abscesses are even all the way to the bottom, because syphilis presses on the intestines.
Et li signes est quant c’est de la section dou syfac, qu’elle fait venir a l’encomencement dolor soudaine, et est li apostemes divers apparans, desoz le cuir pres, et c’est por l’issue de l’intestine et le cors au defuer dou syfac.	And the signs are that it is of the section of the syphilis, that it brings sudden pain at the beginning, and the abscesses appear various, under the skin close by, and it is due to the exit of the intestine and the body from the syphilis.
Et aucune fois dessent li cirbes avec l’intestine, et est retenus enqui, et fait grant dolor soffrir au malaide, meismement quant il est pressez.	And sometimes the stones descend with the intestine, and are retained inside, and cause great pain for the patient, especially when they are pressed.
Et en ces cures de fer a paor, por coi il s’en covient eschuir.	And in these treatments of iron, there is fear, because of which one should abstain from it.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que tu comande ou malaide qu’il ramoine l’intestine a sa main au dedens en la plaie, s’il i puet rentreir;	And the way to do this treatment is to instruct the patient to pull the intestine into his hand inside the wound, if he can reach it;
puis soit sovinez sus son col. entre tes mains, et lieve les cuixes;	then let him be bent forward over his neck between your hands, and press his thighs.
puis estent le keur au desus, et cope tout le cuir des coions dou lonc;	then the chest is pressed down and all the skin of the testicles from above is cut away
puis boute dedens les leivres de la taille uncines selonc ceu que tu en as mestier por ovrir la plaie, et soit telz que li oes em puist issir;	then insert hooks into the loins according to what you need in order to open the wound, and it should be such that the bile can come out.
puis escorche lou syfac que est desoz lou cuir des coions, tant que li blans syfac dur soit descovers de toutes pars;	then scrape off the scrotum skin that is under the testicle skin, until the white, hard scrotum is uncovered all around.
puis boute ton doi indice en ceu qui enseut lou coion, en ceu qui est entre lou blanc syfac qui est desoz lou cuir de l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac,	then put your index finger in the one that follows the anus, in what is between the white membrane which is under the egg's shell, and between the second membrane
et depart ceu qui est derrier l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac; et pues muef a la main destre dedens lou keur des coions, et estent lou blanc syfac en haut a ta main senestre, et lieve l’uef a tout lou syfac devers la taille;	and separate what is behind the egg, and between the second membrane; and then move your right hand inside the anus, and hold the white membrane upwards in your left hand, and lift the egg away from all the membrane towards the waist;
et comande au ministre qu’il estende l’uef en haut, et deslie ceu qui est aers derrier le liement;	and instruct the assistant to extend the egg upwards, and loosen what is air behind the bowel;
et quier a tes dois s’il a point de l’intestine envoloupeit ou blanc syfac dur, et se tu en trueves aucune chose, si le boute au ventre desoz;	and feel with your fingers if there is any intestinal wrapper or hard white membrane, and if you find anything, then put it back into the belly underneath;
puis pren une aguille ou il ait .i. gros fil fait de .x. filz, et la boute en la derriere partie dou syfac, qui est aprés lou cuir des coions; aprés la taille, puis cope les chiés qui apperent des filz, tant qu’il i ait .iiij. filz;	take a needle with .i. large thread made of .x. threads, and insert it into the rear part of the scrotum, which is after the skin of the testicles; after the scrotum, then tie the threads that appear, so that there are .iiij. threads;
puis les assemble l’un sus l’autre en maniere de croix, et en lie lou syfac, dont nos avons dit qui est desoz lou cuir des coions, d’un fort liien de .ij. pars;	then tie them one above the other in the shape of a cross, and bind the scrotum, of which we have spoken and is under the skin of the testicles, with a strong ligature of 2 parts;
puis envoloupe les chiés des filz, et les lie forment de .ij. pars, si que nuls des vasselz que les norrissent ne puissent entrer en ous, que aposteme chaus n’i viegne;	then wrap the threads around the scrotum and tie them tightly in a figure-eight shape, so that none of the vessels that nourish it can enter, so that no abscess can form there;
et met derechief le liien selonc le premier liien lonc .ij. dois de celui, et aprés ces .ij. liiens laisse dou syfac qui est desoz lou keur des coions le grant d’un doi;	and cut the ligature according to the first long ligature in 2 parts of that one, and after those 2 ligatures, leave the scrotum which is under the heart of the testicles with the large part of a finger;
et aprés tout l’autre selonc la rondesce que li euf porte; puis cope en la partie qui est desoz le cuir des coions, tant qui li sans corre, et li bowe, si com nos avons dit ci devant;	and then the other according to the roundness that the eye carries; then press in the part which is under the skin of the testicles, as far as the blood flows, and the bowels, as we have said before;
puis amenistre laine moillie en oile, et met em plaies, et i amenistre le liien que nos avons dit.	then apply wool moistened in oil, and place it on the wounds, and then apply the ligature that we have described.
Et aucune fois est cauterizez li blans syfac que nos avons dit, aprés l’incision, par doutance de decorrement de sanc.	And sometimes the white syphilis that we have mentioned is cauterized after the incision, due to fear of blood flow.
Car ce avient maintes fois, et laisse le liien tant qu’il chiece per lui; et s’il tarde au cheoir, si soit arosez d’aigue chaude, et met sus ceu que nos avons dit, tant qu’il chiece;	For it happens many times, and they leave the ligature in place until it falls off; and if it takes a long time to fall off, then use warm water, and apply what we have said until it falls off;
puis cure la plaie d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	then treat the wound with another treatment until it is completely healed.
de hernie carnouse	of fleshy hernia
En ceste ramice ne vis je onques nul qui osast faire la cure par fer.	In this branch, I have never seen anyone dare to perform the cure with iron.
Et li ancien dirent qu’ele est faite si com li ramice qui est ensamble la vis, en teil maniere que tu lie les vasselz, aprés la taille sus ous legierement au desoz;	And the ancients said that it is done in the same way as the ramifice which is together with the vein, in such a way that you ligature the vessels, after cutting it above gently from below;
puis cope em mi, et cure l’aposteme de ceu qui oevre, tant que li vasselz chient; et le cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	then press on it, and open the abscess of whoever is affected, until the vessels burst; and treat it as we have said, until he is healed.
Aucune fois vient routure ens angres, si com nos avons dit, et apert li leus; et ne dessent nulz des intestines as coions, et s’il en i dessent, c’est poc, et repaire toutes houres;	Sometimes there is a rupture in the intestines, as we have said, and the orifice opens; but no intestines protrude through it, and if they do, it is very little, and it can be repaired at any time;
et toutevoie s’il demoure trop en cest point, si croit li plaie ou syphac, tant que li intestine dessent;	but if he stays too long in this condition, the hernia grows, until the intestines protrude;
et ceu avient par l’estension dou syfac qui est as angres, si com nos avons dit, car il est estendus, puis est mollifiez et enflez li leus et apert;	and this happens because of the extension of the hernia, as we have said, for it is extended, then it becomes soft and swollen, and the orifice opens;
et li cure si est par cautere, si com nos avons devant dit; et aucune fois est curee par fer en ceste maniere:	and the treatment is by cautery, as we have said before; and sometimes it is treated with iron in this way:
et est que li malaides gise sovin sus son dos entre tes mains, puis cope le leu de la routure enfleit dou large selonc la quantiteit de .iij. dois;	and the patient lies on his back between your hands, then you press the site of the fracture gently with the broad end of a spoon according to the quantity of three eggs;
et puis estrai le syfac qui est desoz le cuir que l’ensuet, puis pren lou rait et lou met sor le leu apparant dou syfac;	then pull out the pus sac which is under the skin, then take the thread and place it over the visible spot of the pus sac;
et lou presse au parfont dou ventre, puis cout les .ij. leus apparans dou syfac sus lou chief dou rait, et cout l’un et l’autre;	and press deeply into the abdomen, then tie off the two visible spots of the pus sac on the head of the thread, and tie one and then the other;
puis estrai le chief dou rait, et ne coper point dou syfac ne n’estendre l’uef n’autre chose, si com je t’ai fait savoir en la cure de la ramice des intestines;	then pull the head of the vein, and do not cover it with syrup or extend the wound or anything else, as I have made you aware in the treatment of a rupture of the intestines;
puis le cure par la cure des plaies. Et quant tu copes les filz, si le mundefie et cure la plaie, tant qu’elle soit sanee.	then treat it according to the treatment of wounds. And when you bandage the threads, clean and treat the wound until it heals.
Li syfac est constrains, et n’a point d’apparance en la routure, et li cauteres est muedres en cest leu, et plus prochiens a salut.	Syrup is constricting and has no appearance in bleeding, and cautery is more beneficial and closer to healing.
de l’amollissement dou cuir des coions	of the softening of the skin of the testicles
Maintes fois est amollis li cuirs des coions en aucuns homes, por ceu que les chars que sont dedens sont mollifiees, et est lait a veoir; et est mestier, quant on le vuet curer, c’on faice gesir lou malaide sus son dos, et li cope le cuir qui est mollifiez sus le cuir natureil; puis assemble les .ij. levres a une costure, et se tu vues, cout premier la superfluiteit dou cuir mollifiiez a .iij. costures ou .iiij. fermement; puis cope entre les costures, et lou cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez, et chient li fil.	Many times the skin of the scrotum becomes soft in some men because the testicles inside are softened, and it appears milky white; and when one wishes to treat it, they must make the patient lie on his back, and cut the softened skin on top of the natural skin; then sew the two lips together with a single stitch, and if you see, close the superfluity of the softened skin with three or four stitches firmly; then cut between the stitches, and treat it as other wounds until it heals, and cut the thread.
dou chastrement	of chastisement
Saiches que chastremens est escomeniez en nostre loi, et por ceu il me plairoit que je n’en parlasse mie en cest livre; et n’est necessaires fuer que por .ij. manieres: dont l’une est que li mires en saiche respondre quant on li demandera, et en saiche la cure; et li autre, por ceu que nos avons sovent mestier de chastrement d’aucunes bestes por nos aidier, si com de bouc et de mouton et de chait et d’autres bestes. Je dis donques que chastremens est fais selonc .ij. manieres: ou par atraction, ou par fendure.  En celle que nos faisons par attraction, faisons nos seoir la beste en aigue chaude, tant que li coion soient mollifiez et pendant; puis les preing a ta main, tant qu’il soient remis et que tu ne les sentes plus.  Du chastrement de taille: covient que tu teignes la beste, et li presse le cuir des coions a ta main senestre, puis lie le suspensoire, et cope sus chescun oef a .i. cop, quant tu les avras bien escorchiez; et i laisse aucun poc dou syfac et lou subtil syfac qui est sor les vasselz; et ceste maniere de chastrement est muedre que cele qui est faite par attraction, por ceu que a l’atraction demoure par aventure aucune chose des coions, par coi li beste desire luxure; puis cure la plaie tant qu’ele soit sanee.	Do you know that chastisement is prohibited by our law, and because of this, I would prefer not to discuss it in this book; and it is only necessary for two reasons: one is so that the surgeon knows how to respond when asked, and knows how to treat it; and the other is because we often need to use chastisement on certain animals to help us, such as bulls, rams, and horses. I say then that chastisement is done in two ways: by attraction or by cutting. With the method of attraction, we make the animal sit in warm water until the testicles are softened and dangling; then squeeze them in your hand until they are back in place and you no longer feel them. For the method of cutting: tie the animal down, and cut the skin of the scrotum with your left hand, then cut each testicle open at the middle, once you have well-scalded them; and leave some pus and the thin membrane that covers the vessels; this method of chastisement is better than the one done by attraction, because with attraction, something from the testicles might remain, causing the animal to desire lust; then treat the wound until it heals.
des hermofrodites	of hermaphrodites
Hermofrodie est selonc .ij. manieres as homes: l’une si est que entre les .ij. coions apert ausi com li figure de la nature d’une femme, ou il ait poil, et aucunes fois en cort li urine.  Et li autre maniere si est en femmes, et ait sus lou poignil ausi com une verge et .ij. coions.  Et li cure de l’ome et de la fame si est que tu copes les chars ajostees toutes, et les cure si com autres plaies; en la seconde maniere, des homes dont li urine saut par lou cuir des coions, si n’a point de cure.	There are two kinds of hermaphrodites: one is male, but between their legs it is open like a woman's vagina, with pubic hair, and sometimes they even ejaculate.  The other is female, with a penis on the scrotum, and both testicles and ovaries.  In the first kind, you treat them like any other wound; in the second kind, those who urinate through the skin of their scrotum cannot be cured.
de la tentigene	of the tetter
Tentigene est une chars ajostee sus la partie natureil, tant qu’elle est trop laide a veoir; et aucunes femmes l’ont ausi grant com une main, et c’est li cure. Il covient que tu teignes la superfluiteit de la tentigene a ta main ou as oncines, et la cope legierement; et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que decorremens de sanc n’i viegne, puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez; et a une autre char que naist a la bouche de la marris, et l’emple, et par aventure saut fuer, et est selonc la semblance d’une kowe, et por ceu l’apelerent li ancien «maladie kowee». Si covient que tu la copes, si com nos avons dit la tentigene, et la cure tant qu’elle soit sanee.	Tetter is a skin disease that causes ugly sores on the body; some women have it as large as a hand, and that is the cure. You must cut away the excess skin of the tetter with your hand or fingernails, but not too deeply so that bleeding occurs, and then cure the sore with another sore until it is healed. There is also a sore that arises in the mouth, which looks like a cow's udder, and they call it the "cow disease". You must cut this as you would the tetter, and then cure it once it is healed.
de erratique	of erratics
Erratique si est quant li nature de la femme n’est mie percie, ou li pertus est petis; et est naturez par naissance, ou accidens par maladie que venue i est; ou c’est par char ajostee, ou dou syfac subtil ou espés, et est fais em parfont en la marris, ou en costez, ou desoz, ou que soit; et deffent le concevoir, et l’enfantement, et par aventure les flors a avoir; et li connoissance de ceu si est par le regart de la baile. Se li estoupemens est prochiens apparans, si quier a tes dois ou au rait. S’il est dou syfac subtil, et il est prochiens as .ij. leivres, si te haste, et la ront ensi: met tes .ij. dois indices ensamble, et li femme soit sus son dos, espandues ses jambes; puis estent les .ij. leivres forment, tant que li subtilz syfac soit rons, et soit overs li estoupemens; puis pren laine, et la moille en oile, et la met sus le leu, et gise li femme a home chescun jor, si qu’il ne puist souder. Et se li syfac est dur et espés, si covient que tu lou copes au spatumile semblant a foille de mirte. Se li estoupemens est de char nee, si la sospent a l’oncine et la cope; et aies les medicines estainchans sanc, si com acaice, sanc de dragon, encens, ensamble abun d’uef; puis amenistre une caine de plonc large, si que li plaie ne puisse souder; et ensi soit longement, et li amenistre une tente de lin sec; puis soit curez d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.  Et quant en la marris vient char nee, si la covient coper selonc ceste maniere, se ce n’est apostemes enchancrez. Car a l’aposteme enchancreit qui est en la marris, ne doit on touchier de feir.
