des emorroides	of hemorrhoids
Emorroydes sont overtures de voines dont sans cort acostumeement, et quant les emorroydes sont vielles si devienent thelul; et nos avons jai dit en la division les semblances d’aus, et les signes, et je dirai ci celles qui resoivent curation. Je di que les emorroides et li thelul, quant il sont em parfont en la marris, et il n’aperent au sentir, si n’est mie li cure par fer. Cil qui sont a la bouche de la marris, c’on puet sentir, sont cil c’on puet curer. Il covient donques que tu mettes la femme en une maison froide, puis estent l’altelul as tenailles, et le cope en ses racines, puis poudre sus medicines restraignans sanc, si com acaice et sanc de dragon et encens, et semblans choses; puis boute ses piez a la paroit une houre, puis la met en aigue froide; et se decorremens de sanc i vient, si la fai seoir en une decoction de sumac et d’escorce de pomes grenates et de gales et de semblans choses, et puis pren farine d’orge, et la confis avec miel et aisil, et en fai .i. emplaustre sus son dos. Et se il estainche, c’est boin. Se ceu non, se li fai aerdre ventouses au dos et as mameles sens ferir; puis pren lainne, et la moille en jus de plantain ou en jus d’aglentier avec vin viel, et fai aerdre au leu.  Et quant li aposteme repose, si cure lou leu d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez; et celle qui est apelee «albathir» est rouge, et est semblans a .i. chief aspre, si le covient coper si com j’ai dit le thelul; et puis lou cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	Hemorrhoids are opened veins from which blood flows freely, and when hemorrhoids are old, they become thrombosed; and we have already described their appearances, signs, and treatments in a previous section. I said that both hemorrhoids and thrombosed hemorrhoids, when they are fully formed inside the anus, and do not respond to treatment with medication, can only be cured by surgery using iron instruments. Those that can be felt at the entrance of the anus can be treated. Therefore, one should place the patient in a cool room, then cut off the hemorrhoids with tweezers, and cauterize their roots with a mixture of powdered astringent medications such as acacia and dragon's blood incense, and similar substances; then bind her feet to the wall for an hour, and then submerge her in cold water. If there is any bleeding, she should sit in a decoction made from sumac, pomegranate bark, galls, and similar substances. Then take barley flour, mix it with honey and garlic, and apply it as a poultice to her back. If this stops the bleeding, that is good. If not, apply leeches to the back and breasts without using iron instruments; then take wool, soak it in plantain juice or aglet leaf juice mixed with old wine, and apply it to the affected area. Once the abscess has drained, treat the wound with ointment until it heals. The one called 'albathir' is red and resembles a hard lump, so it should be treated as I have described for thrombosed hemorrhoids; then cure it until it is healed.
des apostemes de la marris	Here is the translation of the provided text:
Maintes manieres d’aposteme vienent en la marris, si com chancre et aposteme pierous et herpes et estiomenes et fistules et emorroides et aposteme chaut, et plusors autres maladies que j’ai dit en la division. Il covient donques que je die en cest traitier l’aposteme chaut qui vient en la marris, qui n’est mie des apostemes que coillent bowe; et se tu vues savoir l’ovraige de fer, si regarde se li apostemes est agus en l’encomencement de sa venue, et plain de chalor et de fievre, et s’il devient rouge se tu le pues veoir.  Adonques ne te haster mie de percier, mais lou fais meurer tant que li dolor soit apaisie; et puis fai seoir lou malaide sus .i. siege, et ait .ij. petis sieges ou il se cline, et apoie sus son dos et assemble ses piez as parties defuer la jambe; et soient ses cuixes espandues, et mette ses braz desoz ses genous, et les lie bien d’un boin liien; puis succe li baille devers lou destre costeit, et i amenistre l’estrument dont on oevre la bouche de la marris, de coi ci aprés vient li forme; et covient que quant tu i vues amenistrer cest estrument, que tu fiches le rait premier ens por savoir la parfondeté de la marris, si que ceu qui entre ens de l’estrument n’i viegne plus em parfont qu’il ne doit, et qu’il ne blece la malaide; et se li estrumens est plus grans, si covient covrir la parfondesce de la marris de drapelz, si que li estrumens ne li grieve; et covient qu’il mette le cornet de l’estrument au desus, et qu’il teigne l’estrument. Et quant li apostemes apert, et on lou fent a la main mol, si le covient coper au chief, au spatumile leit; et quant li bowe est vuidie, si covient que tu mettes en la plaie tentes moillies en oile roset, ou en oile vert sec; et met la tente fuer de la plaie au parfont de la marris, et met par defuer sus la marris et sus le poignil lainne nette moillie en aigue ou malves soient cuites; puis le cure aprés .ij. jors d’oignement avenant a ceu, tant qu’il soit sanez; et aucune fois leve on la marris et la plaie par clistere d’aigue et de miel, et puis d’aigue ou racines de lis et aristologe longe soient cuites; puis reveigne a l’oignement.  Et se li plaie est reponue en la marris, si covient que tu te gardes de cuire de fer, mais cure la si com nos avons dit en la division.	There are many types of abscesses that can form in the anus, including sores, piercings, herpes, fistulas, hemorrhoids, and hot abscesses, as well as several others that I have described in a previous section. Therefore, I will now describe in this treatise the hot abscess that forms in the anus, which is not the same as the one that occurs in the bowels. If you want to know how to use the instrument, examine whether the abscess is suppurating at the beginning of its formation, and if it is accompanied by heat and fever, and if it turns red when you look at it. Then, do not rush to pierce it, but let the pain subside first; then, have the patient sit on a chair with two small seats for leaning, one against the back and one against the legs, and let the buttocks be spread apart, and place the arms under the knees, and tie them securely with a good rope. Then, suck the orifice towards the right side, and insert the instrument used to open the anus, so that you can determine the depth of the anus and ensure that the instrument does not go in too deep and harm the patient. If the instrument is larger, cover the depth of the anus with cloth so that it is not uncomfortable, and place the tip of the instrument inside, and then draw it out. When the abscess breaks open and the bowels are released, apply moist tents soaked in rose oil or green oil to the wound, pushing the tent into the anus and placing linen soaked in water or malva flowers over the anus and around the perineum. Then treat the wound with ointment for two days, and then raise the anus and the wound using a clyster of water and honey, and then water infused with lily roots and aristolochia. Return to treating the wound with ointment. If the wound has drained inside the anus, refrain from using heat, but treat it as we have described earlier.
de l’enfantement	of childbirth
Mestier est premier a la baile qu’elle conoisse la figure de l’enfantement natureil, et li signes si est quant tu vois la femme apresser aval, et desire odorer l’ar: adonques se haste li enfes de fuer issir; adonc saiches que cil enfantemens est selonc la figure natureil, et est li issue soz son chief, et li secondine avec lui; et quant tu vois ces signes, si covient presser legierement son ventre, si que li enfes isse tost; car quant il dessent sus son chief, si ist li secondine avec lui, et est mondee li marris de ses superfluitez par bone mundification; et cist qui vient autrement ne vient mie naturelment. Car il vient aucune fois sus ses piez, et vient fuer li cors ou li chiés, et les mains, ou il vient sus son ventre, ou sovin, et est convertis par aventure sor son col, et par autres figures malvaises; si est mestier a la baile qu’elle soit saige et subtilz en ces choses, et se warse d’error et de decevement, et je vos mostrerai toutes les figures coment on li doit aidier.	It is necessary for the midwife to know the natural form of childbirth and its signs; when you see a woman breathing quickly and desiring to smell flowers, then hasten the child's exit; then you can tell that this childbirth follows nature, with the placenta emerging after the child, and the mother's excess fluids are expelled through proper cleansing; anything different is not natural. Sometimes the baby emerges feet first, or emerges from the body, arms, or abdomen, and sometimes it gets twisted onto its neck or other unnatural positions. The midwife must be wise and skilled in these matters, aware of errors and deceptions, and I will show you how to assist in all situations.
Se li enfes vient sus son chief par issue natureil, et li femme enfante griement, et li vertus de li est foible, si la fai seoir sus une selle, ou les femmes la tienent; et arose sa nature d’oile ou fenugreic soit cuit, et puis boute li baile entre ses dois le petit spatumile dont ci est li forme:	If the baby emerges head-first through a natural birth canal, and the mother gives birth painfully with weak contractions, then seat her on a stool or have other women support her. Boil a mixture of oil and fenugreek, and then use a small spatula (as described below) to gently apply it:
et fende la secondine, et cope a son ungle tant que li moistors qui est ens corre fuers; et preint lou ventre de la femme tant que li enfes dessende, et s’il ne dessent, si covient clisterizer la femme de muscillaige de fenugrec avec oile de sisament; puis la fai preindre et esternuer de condisi, et tien sa bouche et son neis une houre: si istra maintenant l’enfes.Et se les .ij. mains issent fuer, si covient que tu les ramoinne legierement poc et poc; et s’elles n’i puent entrer, si met la femme sus .i. siege, et li lieve les piés en haut; puis deboute le siege sus terre, et teigne on la femme, qu’elle ne chiece au deboutement; et se li mains n’i puet entrer, et li enfes muert, si li cope les mains au couteil qui est ci devant mis, et estrai l’enfant, et ramoine igalment.	and split the placenta, and press her fingernails into her until the moisture that is within flows out; and squeeze her belly so that the baby descends, and if it doesn't descend, then cleanse the woman with a poultice of ground fenugreek mixed with sisament oil; then make her sneeze and cough from the spice mixture, and hold her mouth and nose for an hour: then the baby will emerge. And if both hands come out, then gently pull them back in little by little; and if they can't go in, then sit the woman on a chair, and raise her feet up; then stand the chair on the ground, and lean her forward so she is not bent over; and if the hands still can't go in, and the baby dies, then grasp the hands at the knuckles as described before, and pull out the child, and proceed likewise.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses piez	of the birth of a child on its feet
Quant li enfes vient sus ses piez, si lou covient bouter en haut;	When the child is born standing, it should be turned over;
et puis le torne poc et poc, tant qu’il soit igalz;	and then turn him slowly and gently until he is straight;
puis preigne .i. des piez et l’estende poc et poc.	then grab one of his feet and stretch it out slowly.
Cant il saut jusc’as cuixes, si la comande a preindre, et la fai esternuer de condisi;	When it jumps up to the armpit, instruct it to grab hold, and make it sneeze from its condition;
si saut fuer, se Deus vuet.	if it jumps out, God willing.
Et s’il n’ist fuer si com nos avons dit, si le torne poc et poc, tant qu’il soit selonc la figure natureil.	And if it does not jump out as we have said, then move it little by little, until it is in its natural position.
Car adonques ist il legierement.	For then it will be easy.
Et s’il ne vient fuer si com nos avons dit, si pren muscillaige de altee, et oile de sisament, et gomme fondue, et broie tout en .i. mortier;	And if it does not come out as we have said, then take musk, and oil of sarsaparilla, and melted gum, and grind them all in a mortar;
et met sus la nature de la femme dedens et defuer cest oignement,	and put it on the woman's nature inside and smear this ointment,
puis la fai seoir en aigue tede jusque desoz les costelz;	then let her sit in warm water up to her ribs;
et quant elle est moillifie desoz, se li fai .i. coliere de mirre, et li met desoz, et li laisse une houre;	and when she is moistened underneath, make her a collar of myrrh and put it on her, and leave it for an hour;
puis la fai seoir sus .i. siege, puis la fai esternuer et estraint sa bouche et son neis, et li preint le ventre legierement, car li enfes saut maintenant.	then have her sit on a chair, then make her sneeze and constrict her mouth and nose, and gently press her belly, for the child will jump now.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses genous	of the child's delivery onto his knees
Quant li enfes vient en ceste forme, si i mette li baile ses mains poc et poc;	When the child comes in this way, he puts his hands on it little by little.
puis soit sovinee sus son col, et li pendent li piez aval, et soit gisans sor .i. lit;	then he is placed on his back, and his legs hang down, and he lies on a bed.

de l’issue de l’enfant qui vient dou large une main pendant	of the infant's exit, which should be about one hand wide
I covient engignier a ramener la main:	One must try to bring back the hand:
s’on ne la puet ramener, si fai lever la femme, et aler;	if one cannot, then have the woman stand up and walk;

et s’elle n’enfante, si la fai seoir sus .i. siege, puis estudie au rameneir la main;	and if she does not give birth, then have her sit on a seat, then study to bring the hand back;
et ewe l’enfant selonc la figure natureil, et la fai esternuer, et li comande qu’elle se preigne tant que li enfes isse fuer.	and turn the child according to its natural position, and have her sneeze, and command her to press until the baby comes out.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus son col, et ait espandues ses mains, et sa faice tornee devers lou dos sa mere	from the child's exit onto its neck, and have her hands spread out, and her face turned towards her mother's back
I covient que li baile teigne sa main, puis le torne poc et poc, et l’ewe legierement;	I must twist her hand, then turn it little by little, and hold it gently;
et quant il est igalz, si met sus la nature muscillaige de altee et oile, si com nos avons dit, puis li comande qu’elle se mueve poc et poc;	and when it is even, he puts on the musselage of arnica and oil, as we have said, then he commands that it moves little by little.
et quant tu avras ce fait, si la fai seoir sus .i. siege, et li comande k’elle se preigne; et la fai esternuer.	and when you have done this, make her sit on a seat, and command that she sneezes, and make her sneeze.
de ceste meisme maniere a tout la secondine	in the same way for all of the afterbirth
Quant il vient fuer en ceste maniere a tout la secondine, si cope la secondine a ton ungle, tant que li moistors soit vuidie;	When it comes out in this way to all of the afterbirth, then scrape the afterbirth with your fingernail until the moisture is evacuated;
et se li enfes pent sus sa faice et sus son col, si la cope des la boude, qu’elle ne soit retenue, et muere li enfes;	and if the child lies on its face and on its neck, then the mother will smother it, and the child will die.
puis boute l’enfant dedens, tant que tu l’aies mis si com il covient, et comande a la femme qu’elle se preigne aucune fois:	then put the child inside, so that you have placed him as it should be, and instruct the woman to hold on for a while:
adonques si istra legierement.	then if he is released easily.
de l’issue des gemelz	of the issue of twins
Saiches que gemeil naissent maintes fois, et aucune fois en naissent .iij. ou .iiij.; et ceu n’est mie estrainge chose, et poc avient.	Know that twins are often born, and sometimes triplets or quadruplets; and this is not a strange thing, but it happens seldom.
Dui sont estrainge chose, et ne vivent mie, se poc nom;	Twins are a strange thing, and they do not live long if they are few in number.
je sai ceu, qu’il soient multipliiet, et sont desevrez par lou syfac qui les devise, qui est liiez a la boude;	I know that when they are multiplied and separated by the placenta, which is attached to the womb,
et aucune fois issent ausi naturelment com uns tous sous, si com nos avons dit.	and sometimes they issue naturally just like one child, as we have said.
Et s’il issent griement, si la cure si com nos avons dit, et soit li baile subtilz, et faice tost et legierement ceu qu’elle fait;	And if they grow quickly, then the treatment as we have said, and let the nurse be subtle, and do quickly and lightly what she does;
et faice ensi com il vaut mues a salut.	and do thus as it benefits to health.
de plusors enfans	of many children
Aucune fois sont formez en la marris .i. ou .ij. ou .iij. ou .iiij. ou .v. ou .vj. ou .vij., ou plusors jusc’a .xv., et sont tout formeit en forme d’enfant par le mesurement dou saige glorious,	Sometimes they are formed in the womb as 1 or 2 or 3 or 4 or 5 or more up to 15, and they are all shaped like children according to the measurement of the glorified Sage
et couvient que li baile saiche tout ceu, car par aventure semblans chose li avient;	and it is necessary for the surgeon to know all this, because a similar thing might happen to him;
si faice selonc ceu qu’il covient.	then act according to what is appropriate.
de l’enfant mort	of the dead child
Quant tu cures la femme de l’enfant mort ou ventre, si com j’ai dit en la division, et il ne vient fuers, et tu es constrains d’ovraige de mains;	When you are treating a woman of a stillborn child or of a pregnancy, as I have said in the previous section, and there is no sign of life, and you are forced to perform an operation with your hands;
si covient que tu saiches se li femme est de saine vertut, et n’ait accident ou elle ait paor de mort;	if you should know whether a woman is of healthy disposition, and does not have an accident or fear of death;
si covient que li femme soit sovinee sus son dos, et soit ses chiés enclins aval, et les jambes levees;	if the woman should be laid on her back, with her hips tilted down, and her legs raised;
et li ministre la teigne de .ij. pars, ou elle soit liie au lit si qu’elle ne soit traite au dessendement de l’enfant;	and apply the ointment to .10 parts, or she lies in bed so that she is not treated for childbirth;
puis frotez la bouche de la marris d’oiles moistes avec muscillaige de altee et de fenugrec et semence de lin, puis oigne li baile ses mains de ces oiles et de ces muscillaiges;	then rub the mouth of the mother with moist oils mixed with mustard seed and fenugreek and flax seed, then anoint the baby's hands with these oils and musk;
puis les boute en la marris legierement, puis quiere .i. leu ou elle boute les oncines que soient covenaubles a ceu,	then press them gently, then bring .I. [the instrument] to the place where they are biting, which is suitable for this,
et pren warde se li enfes est apparilliez qu’il dessende sus son chief;	and be careful that the child is dressed so that it does not descend onto its head;
si fiche les oncines en ses eulz ou en son col ou en sa bouche ou en som palais ou desoz la barbe ou en la forcele ou pres des costez,	if they bite their fingers in their eyes or in their throat or in their mouth or under the beard or in the armpit or near the sides,
et se li dessendemens est sus piez, se li fiche ou poignil et as costes moienes;	and if the swelling is on the feet, put the instrument or the finger and middle fingers;
et covient qu’il teigne l’oncine a sa main destre, et mette la corbeure entre ses dois de la senestre main, et li boute a tout sa main legierement, et fiche l’oncine en aucun de ces leus que nos avons dit, tant qu’il viegne a la chose vuide;	and he should dye the nail on his right hand, and place the bowstring between the fingers of his left hand, and wind it around his whole hand lightly, and insert the nail into one of the holes we have mentioned, so that it reaches the hollow;
et c’est li forme de l’oncine:	and this is how the nail should be shaped:
puis fiche encontre .i. autre oncine, ou le tier se tu en as mestier, si que li estractions soit igalz;	then insert another nail, or a third one if you need it, so that the extractions are even;
et puis l’estent igalment en movant d’une part et d’autre, por mues issir, et soit li oncines dentez por mues tenir, si com ci est li forme:	and then they should be moved evenly from one side to the other, so that the movements come out, and the nails should bite down to hold the movements, just as this shape shows:
Et s’il en demoure une partie, si oigne li baile aucuns de ses dois d’oile, et les boute en celle partie, et traie l’autre partie;	And if some remains, then anoint the joint of one of his fingers with oil and push it into that part and pull on the other.
et s’il en i demoure point, si met cest oncine ou plus haut leu, et fai ceu tant qu’il s’en isse tout fuers.	And if nothing remains, then move this joint higher up and keep doing this until it comes out completely.
Et se l’une mains vient devant l’autre, et il ne puet ramener por l’estreignement,	And if one hand comes before the other, and he cannot bring it back due to the dislocation,
si covient que tu envoloupes sus .i. drapeil, tant qu’il isse tote;	then you must wrap it in .a. cloth, as much as possible.
puis la cope en la jointure de la plante ou au coute, et ensi covient que tu faices en l’autre main, et as .ij. piés.	then cupping on the joint of the palm or the wrist, and so you must do with the other hand, and at the feet.
Et se li chiés de l’enfant est gros et il est estrois en l’issue, ou il ait ou chief aigue assemblee,	And if the child's head is big and it is stuck in the birth canal, or it has an acute pain gathered at the top,
si covient que tu boute le spatumile espinous entre tes dois, et fent le chief et estrai l’aigue;	you must push the thorny spear-like instrument between your fingers, and pierce the head and draw out the pain;
ou tu la ront a l’estrument qui est apelez «almidach», de coi li forme vient avec les estrumens ou chapistre qui est aprés cestui;	or you can use the instrument called "almidach," from which the form comes with the instruments or chapters that follow this one;
et ensi meisme faice se li enfes a grant chief naturelment;	and so the infant is born with a large head naturally;
et puis traie fuer les osses as tenailles,	and then pulls out the bones with tongs,
et se li chiés saut fuer et il estraint a la forcele, si soit fendus, tant que li moistors qui est ou pis issue fuer;	and if the head pops out and is forced, being split, so that the moisture which is in the bottom comes out;
et s’elle ne puet issir, si le cope par pieces au mues que tu pues;	and if it cannot come out, then cut it into pieces as small as you can;
et s’il est enflez au ventre ou desoz les costez, si covient que tu lou perces tant que li moistors corre.	and if he is swollen in the belly or under the ribs, then you must pierce him so that the moisture flows out.
Et se li enfes est sus ses piez, si est li attraction legiere, et li adrecemens a la bouche de la marris est legier.	And if the swelling is on his feet, then the traction is light, and the direction to the mouth of the wound is light.
Et s’il est estrois au ventre ou au pis, si couvient que tu l’estraies a .i. drapeil envoloupeit sus la main;	And if it is swollen in the belly or on the foot, then you must stretch it with .a. cloth wrapped around your hand;
et fent le ventre ou le pis, tant que li moistors qui i est corre;	and pierce the belly or foot, so that the moisture that is in it flows out;
et se li autre membre sont osteit, et li chiez demoure,	and if the other members are paralyzed, and the feet remain,
si boute li baile sa main em parfont de la marris, et le traie jusc’a la bouche de la marris;	then the surgeon should plunge his hand into the wound up to the wound's mouth;
puis i boute .i. oncine ou ij., et le trai fuer;	then he inserts a hook or two, and pulls it out;
et se li bouche de la marris est retrecie por aposteme chaut qui i est venus, si n’i covient mie travillier,	and if the mouth of the wound is narrow due to a hot abscess that has formed there, then one must not work on it,
ains covient amenistrer choses moistes et grasses;	then one must apply moist and fatty substances;
et li amenistre emplaustres, et siece en aigue mollifians et amoistans.	and the administrator should use poultices, and put on warm, softening water.
Et se li enfes est sus son costeit, et tu le pues mettre igal, si amenistre ceu que nos avons dit en l’enfant vif;	And if the child is on its side, and you can get it to lie down, then administer what we have said for a living child;
et s’on nen ait pooir, si lou trai fuer par pieces, et n’i laissier rien de la secondine.	and if one cannot, then cut it into pieces, and leave nothing of the afterbirth.
Et quant tu avras ce fait, se li amenistre ceu que nos avons dit ens apostemes chaus que vienent en la marris;	And when you have done this, if the patient is suffering from those abscesses that come in the sea;
et se decorremens de sanc vient, si soit mise en aigue restraignant, et li amenistre autres cures.	and bloodletting comes, then it should be put in restraining water, and other treatments administered.
Et je vis une femme en cui ventre uns enfes avoit esteit mors, puis consut .i. autre sus celui, et refut mors li autres.	And I saw a woman who had had a dead fetus in her womb, then another was sewn over it, and the other died.
Aprés lonc tens li vint uns apostemes en la boude, et enfla tant qu’il ovrit, et comensa a grant porreture.	After a long time, she got an abscess in her armpit, which swelled up so much that it opened and began to discharge greatly.
je fui apelez a la cure, et i pensai lonc tens, et ne pot soder li plaie.	I was called to the cure, and I thought long and hard, but could not heal the wound.
Je mis sus emplaustre de fort attraction, et en issit uns os, et aprés aucuns jors uns autres.	I applied a strong吸引 plaster, and out came a bone, and after a few days, some more.
Je me mervillai mout, por ceu c’ou ventre n’a point d’os.	I was very wonderstruck, for I see that the belly has no bones.
Si pensai que c’estoit des os d’un enfant mort.	I thought that these were the bones of a dead child.
Je quis la plaie, et en traï mains os, tant que li femme fut em miglior point;	Examine the wound and lay hands on the bones until the woman was in a better state.
et vesquit li femme lonc tens ensi, et issoit adés un poc de bowe dou leu;	and thus the woman lived for a long time, and sometimes a little blood would issue from the wound;
et je n’ai recordeit cest chapistre fuer que por ceu que, quant li maistres trueve une estrainge chose, qu’il i saiche mettre aide.	and I have not recorded this chapter except that whenever masters find something strange, they should know how to apply a remedy.
dou ramener la marris a son leu	to bring the bone back to its place
Ci aprés vient li forme dou pressor, a coi on ewe les livres; et a .ij. tornans as .ij. chiés des .ij. liiens.	Hereafter comes the form of the press, with which one is weaned; and at .ij. turnings at .ij. heads of .ij. strings.
Toutevoie, li cornes soit plus subtilz dou restrictoire, et soit fais de ebene ou de bux;	Nevertheless, the horns are more subtle in the constrictor, and they are made from ivory or boxwood;
et soit li bouche dou fust .i. doi de large, et li marge des arbres .i. doit, et de lonc une palme et demi;	and the mouth of the tube should be one digit wide, and the rim of the tubes one digit, and long one palm and a half;
et enmi les .ij. liemens soient dui ajostemens de cest meisme fust, qui soient fermeit en l’un et en l’autre, de demi palme de lonc ou un poc plus;	and in the .ij. edges are two adjustments of this same tube, which are firmly joined in one and the other, half a palm long or a little more;
et cist dui ajostement sont bouteit en la bouche de la marris por ovrir quant on torne les .ij. cornes.	and these two settings are inserted into the mouth of the wound to open when you turn the two horns.
Une autre forme, a sa semblance plus subtilz et plus legiere, soit faite de fust de ebene ou de bux, selonc la semblance des tenailles;	Another form, with its appearance more subtle and lighter, is made of ebony wood or boxwood, according to the appearance of pliers;
et ait as .ij. chiés .ij. ajostemens, si com tu vois, d’une palme de lonc, et .ij. dois de large;	and has two heads, two settings, as you see, a palm long, and two fingers wide;
et quant tu vues ovrir la marris a tout l’estrument, si fai seoir la femme sor .i. lit, les piez pendant et les jambes overtes,	and when you see the wound opened to all the instrument, then let the woman sit on a bed, feet hanging and legs spread,
puis boute les .ij. ajostemens ajostez ensamble en la marris, et tien le chief de l’estrument desoz entre ses cuixes;	then tie the two pieces of the instrument together at the bottom, and hold the head of the instrument between his legs;
puis oevre ta main a tout l’estrument, si com tu as fait as tenailles igalment, selonc la quantiteit que tu vues ovrir la bouche de la marris, tant que li baile faice ceu qu’elle vuet.	then work your hand on the entire instrument, just as you did with the tongs, according to how much you want to open the mouth of the wound, until the patient does what he wants.
Cist estrument sont tuit sormontez, et sont multiplies lor semblances; et quant li mires les ait apareilliez, tant est plus hastans li oevre, et plus haute as homes por lor quantiteit.	These instruments are all decorated and have many similarities; and when the surgeon prepares them, the work is faster and easier for the patient due to their design.
Si ne despire mie l’estrument que tu ne l’aies apparelliet, car lor necessitez n’est mie escusauble.	Do not be discouraged by the instrument until you have prepared it, for their necessity is inexcusable.
Quant li secondine est retenue a l’enfantement, si covient que tu comandes a la malaide qu’ele reteigne son alaine, et puis la fai esternuer de condisi, et li estraint tes mains a la bouche et au neis;	When the placenta is retained during childbirth, instruct the patient to hold in her breath and then sneeze it out with force, while you press her hands against her mouth and nose.
et s’elle saut per ceu, bien est.	And if she vomits, all the better.
Se ceu non, si prent .i. pot, et fai .i. pertus ou cuvercle, et i met herbes que puissent ovrir la bouche de la marris, si com calament, rue, anis, camomille, cassialigne et centoire;	If not, take a pot and make an opening in the cover, and place herbs that can open the mouth of the womb, such as chamomile, fennel, anise, and marjoram.
toutes ces herbes, ou aucunes d’eles, soient cuites ou pot en aigue sus le feu; puis met une caine ou pertus dou pot, et l’autre chief en la bouche de la marris,	All of these herbs, or some of them, are boiled in water over the fire; then place one end of the pot in the mouth of the womb, and the other end in the pot.
et la teigne tant que li vapors viegne dedens la marris; puis la fai esternuer, si com nos avons dit.	and the dye until the vapors come within the marble; then make it sneeze, as we have said.
Si saut li secondine hastanment.	Then let the secondine boil gently.
Et s’elle remaint aprés ceste cure, et n’ist mie fuer, si comande a la baile qu’ele moille sa main senestre en oile de sesement ou en muscillaige de altee, et puis la boute en la nature,	And if it remains after this treatment and is not cured, command the bather to moisten her left hand in sesame oil or in the juice of alder, and then wash it off naturally,
et quiere la secondine; et quant elle l’avra trovee, si la preigne et l’estende poc et poc droitement, si que li marris ne chiece a l’estraction;	and seek out the secondine; and when she has found it, she should squeeze it gently and extend it little by little, so that the marble does not crack;
mais la covient movoir legierement a destre et a senestre, et puis traie; si venra et se desaerdra.	But it must be moved slightly to the right and left, and then pulled; it will come out and be dislocated.
Et se li bouche de la marris est jai estrecie, nos avons dit la cure d’esternuer, et de fumigation des herbes;	And if the mouth of the wound is narrow, we have described the cure for sneezing, and the fuming of herbs;
et s’elle n’ist de tout ceu que nos avons dit, si garde que tu ne foloies au traire;	and if it is not one of those that we have mentioned, then beware of pulling;
mais il couvient que ceu qui est a la bouche de la marris, que tu le lies a la cuixe de la femme, puis la clisterize d’oignement tetrafarmaçon;	but it is necessary for the person at the mouth of the wound to tie it to the woman's thigh, then cleanse with a four-drug ointment;
si la porrira et remettra, et venra fuer; mais toutevoie, quant elle porrist si en vient male odor au stomac et au chief, et blece la malaide.	if she can, then she will; but even so, when she does, there is a bad smell in the stomach and head, and it hurts the patient.
Si covient donques fumigations covenaubles a ceu: aucun des anciens ont esproveit fumigation de cresson et de figues seches.	So, therefore, suitable fumigations are necessary: some of the ancients have tried fumigation with watercress and dried figs.
Li forme de l’estrument a coi on fumige la femme a la retenue des flors et de la secondine si est ceste:	The shape of the instrument with which one smokes out the woman in retention of flowers and secundines, if it is this:
Et est de voirre semblant a une caine, et met on le chief subtil en la nature, et les chiés larges sus le feu;	And it is made of glass like a cane, and one puts the small end in the nature, and the wide ends above the fire;
et soit li fumigations sus les charbons, et la teigne tant qu’elle soit gastee, et rencomence une autre.	and have the fuming done over the coals, and the pestilence until it is wasted, and start another one.
de percier lou fondement	to pierce the foundation
Maint enfant naissent qui n’ont mie le fondement perciet, ains l’ait estoupeit uns subtilz syfac:	Many children are born without their fundaments pierced; instead, they have a thin, subtle membrane.
si covient donques a la baile qu’ele perce celui syfac a son doit, et ne lou perce mie de spatumile agut, et garse le lacement qu’elle ne le touche;	therefore, the midwife should pierce that membrane gently with her finger and not with a sharp instrument, and she should be careful not to break it;
puis met sus lainne moillie en vin et en oile, puis la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	then put on wet linen with wine and oil, then the ointment until it is healed.
Et se tu doutes qu’il ne restoupe, si met ou pertus une caine de plonc, et li laisse mains jors, et soit ostee quant li enfes vuet aler en chambres.	And if you doubt that it will heal, put a wooden rod in the wound and leave it for several days, then remove it when the child wants to walk around.
Et aucune fois vient cist estoupemens de soudement de plaie ou d’aposteme; si covient coper celui soudement: si soit curez, si com nos avons dit de la caine de plonc.	And sometimes this clotting comes suddenly from a wound or an abscess; then it must be covered suddenly: then it should be treated, as we have said, with a rod of pine.
de la fistule dou fondement	from the fistula in the fundament
Fistules qui vienent desoz le fondement sont nodation, et groissor que vienent delez lou fondement defuer, ou en l’espaice des .ij. parties,	Fistulas that come from under the anus are nodular and grow larger than those that come out of the anus or in the space between the two parts.
si a une fistule ou plusors; et quant celle nodation est anciene, si aoeuvre, et encort moistor awouse blainche ou subtilz bowe,	If there is one fistula or more; and when that nodule becomes old, it opens up and lets out a white moisture or thin pus.
et aucune fois sont ces fistule persans; et sont conues par ceu qu’il en ist ou egestion ou ventositeit quant li malaide fait egestion, et par aventure en saut uns vers.	And sometimes these fistulas are piercing; and they are caused by what comes out of the body through flatulence or wind when the patient belches, and sometimes one pops out.
Et si a fistules que percent jusc’a la vessie, et jusc’a la moitiet de la verge; et parvienent jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, et jusc’a nout de la kowe.	And there are fistulas that pierce all the way to the bladder, and halfway down the penis; and they reach the hip joint and up to the testicles.The following text is a medieval medical treatise written in Old French, around the 12th-13th centuries.
Et ensi conoist on la fistule persant au fondement, et ne mie persant:	And thus one knows a fistula is piercing at the anus, and not piercing:
et est que tu boutes ton doi indice ou fondement, et boute une aguille subtil d’arain ou de fer en la fistule quant il n’i a tortuositeit.	and you should push your index finger or a needle into the anus, and push a thin needle made of bronze or iron into the fistula when it is not tortuous.
Et s’il ait tortuositeit, si i boute une tente de plonc subtil, ou .i. poil de cheval, tant que tu sentes la tente ou le poil a ton doit;	And if it is tortuous, then push in a tent made of thin splint, or a horsehair, until you feel the tent or hair at your finger;
et se tu ne le sens, et il ne vient dou pertus egestion ne ventositeit ne ver, si com nos avons dit:	and if you do not feel it, and there is no discharge or windiness, as we have said;
saiches qu’elle ne perce mie; si te haste dou curer.	So that it does not pierce through, then hasten to treat it.
Et quant li fistule est persans jusc’a la vessie ou jusc’a conduit de l’urine, si en saut li urine, et ne puet soudeir par medicines.	And when the fistula has reached the bladder or urinary tract, and the urine leaks out, and cannot be stopped by medicine.
S’elle est percie jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, si est li tente venans jusc’au leu;	If it has pierced all the way to the hip joint, then the tent will be inserted all the way in;
s’il n’i a tortuositeit et li invention de la dolor entor, si est qu’il en ist adés bowe, et n’i vaut medicine ne soudement par oignement;	if there is twisting and pain in the area around it, then it will be removed, and medicines or salves will not help.
et en ces fistules persans n’a point de cure fuer que labor, et vaniteit des folz mires qui s’en entremettent.	and for these persian ulcers there is no cure other than hard work and the vanity of foolish physicians who meddle in them.
En celle qui n’est mie persans et n’est mie anciene, a esperance de saniteit par fer, si com j’ai esproveit,	For that which is not persian and not old, there is hope of healing through iron, as I have experienced.
et est que li malaides gise entre tes mains sus son dos; et li lieve les jambes jusque sus ses cuixes, et ait ses cuixes enclinees a son ventre;	And the patient lies on his back, and lifts his legs up to his thighs, and has his thighs tilted towards his belly;
puis boute une tente d’arain, ou de plonc s’il i a tortuositeit, tant que tu saiches ou li tente vient.	Then insert a tent of iron, or of lead if there is tortuosity, as far as you know the tent goes.
Se li malaides la sent entor le fondement, si covient que tu i boutes ton doi indice,	If the pain is felt around the anus, you should insert your index finger
se sens adonques que li tente l’ait perciet; et soit descoverte ou tu sens entre ton doit le syfac ou la char, adonques saiches qu’elle est persans;	and once it has pierced the membrane, and you feel an opening between your finger and the flesh, then know that it is perforated;
si n’i travillier mie c’on ne la puet saner.	one cannot work on it without causing harm.
On dist toutevoie c’on em puet bien saner aucuns, mais ce avient poc;	One can still heal some, but this rarely happens;
et li aide c’on i fait, si est c’on eschaufe le cautere subtil selonc la largesce de la fistule, si com il est devant dit;	and one helps it by heating the thin cautery according to the width of the fistula, as has been said before;
et le boute tout chaut en la fistule, tant qu’il viegne delez le fondement; et faice ceu .ij. fois ou .iij., tant que tu saiches que ces chars fautrees soient arses, qui sont semblant a une penne d’oiseil;	and insert it into the fistula all the way to the bottom, and do this 2 or 3 times, until you know that the false growths, which look like an owl feather, are burned;
et puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre, tant que celle chars isse fuer, puis le cure d’oignement enjanrant char et soudant.	and then treat it with moist bandages dipped in butter, until the growths come out, and then treat it with ointment that softens and heals.
S’il est ensi sanez, c’est bien. Se ceu, nom autrement ne puet estre sanez;	If he is healthy, that's good. If not, it cannot be otherwise healed;
et se li tente entre, et ne perce jusc’au doit qui est ou fondement, et a entre ton doi et la tente une coverture espesse de char ou de syfac, et tu vois la fistule a ceu qui enseut la coverture dou keur;	and if it enters the tent and does not penetrate to the bottom which is at the foundation, and between your finger and the tent there is a thick covering of flesh or skin, and you see the fistula following the covering of the heart;
si le cope des l’encomencement de la fistule, et boute adés avant la tente, et pues le cautere aprés, tant qu’il viegne au chief de la tente;	if he cuts at the beginning of the fistula, and then fills it with clay before the tent, and then cauterizes afterwards, until he reaches the top of the tent;
et sera delivré li tente, et cherra; puis mondefie celles chars fautrees que semblent une penne d’oisel, et n’en remaigne niant.	and the tent will be delivered, and will fall; then he should cauterize those false flesh-like things that look like a bird's feather, and nothing will remain.
Et si li sans te vaint, et cort entre toi et l’uevre, si le cauterize de feu ou de medicine ague.	And if the pus flows, and cuts between you and the wound, then cauterize it with fire or with medicine.
Car li cauteres de feu assemble .ij. bones choses: c’est a savoir, l’arsure de ces chars ajostees, et l’esteinchement de sanc et la sechor de la moistor;	For fire cautery brings together two things: the burning of these charred spots, and the stopping of blood and the drying out of moisture.
puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre ou en choz broiez, tant que li leus giete bowe, et isse fuer li chars arse en la bowe;	Then treat tents that are wet with butter or crushed substance until the places ooze, and let the fires burn in the affected areas.
puis cure la plaie des oignemens soudans enjanrans dure char, et sont les medicines seches.	Then treat the wound of swollen, tough, hard pimples with dry remedies.
Car quant il est restoree, si est sanee et ne revient mie.	For when it is restored, it is healed and does not return.
Et se fistule vient jusc’a parfont dou fondement, et est esloigniez dou cors, se li boute ton doi ou fondement, et enquier ceu.	And if a fistula comes all the way from the fundament, and is distant from the body, put your finger in the fundament, and probe it.
Se tu sens la tente, et entre .ij. est li toile ou li syfac ou chars, ou il est pres a percier, si n’i ait fuers que voie de fiance et d’esperance, par l’aministrement de l’une des .iii. manieres:	If you feel the tent, and between the two is the membrane or the syphilis, or it is about to pierce, then do not use force but rather have faith and hope through one of the three methods:
ou tu le cauterizes si com nos avons dit, ou tu le cope jusc’a fons, ou se tu pues si i met tentes et cure si com premier;	either you cauterize it as we have said, or cut it to the bottom, or if you can, put in tents and cure it as before.
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que tu ne coper le tenement qui tient le fondement, et viegne li egestions par lai sens volenteit;	and do not go too deep, lest you cut the tenement that holds the fundament, and let the evacuations come out through there as well.
puis le cure, si com nos avons dit;	then the cure, as we have said;
par aventure si sera sanez, ou tu esloigne celle coverture et la munde puis qu’elle est copee delez lou fondement, ou par tente ou par autre estrument apointé;	by chance if it is healed, or you remove that cover and clean it after it has been cut away from the foundation, or by tent or other pointed instrument;
puis mondefie cele char fautree qui est en la plaie, tant com tu pues;	then mend that broken bone in the wound as best you can;
puis estudie a restorer la plaie, et a demorer la fistule en la partie defuers le fondement: si iert plus legiere chose au malaide.	then work to restore the wound, and to keep the fistula in the part above the foundation: if it is a lighter thing for the patient.
Et aucune fois sont fistules selonc ceste maniere: et est quant tu boutes la tente en la fistule, et elle est ou costeit dou fondement delez lou cuir desus,	And sometimes there are fistulas in this way: and it is when you put the tent in the fistula, and it is on the side near the foundation below the skin above.
si pren une tente percie au chief selonc ceste forme:	take a tent pierced at the tip according to this shape:
Et i boute .i. fil tort en .ij., et boute la tente a tout le fil en la fistule tant qu’il soit au chief.	And he inserts a twisted thread into the tent, and inserts the tent into the fistula all the way to the tip.
S’elle est persans en la marge dou fondement dedens, adonc estrai lou fil de celui pertus, ensi que tu boutes ton doi ou fondement;	If it pierces through the margin near the foundation inside, then pull out the thread from that opening, as you would put your finger into the foundation.
et trai le chief dou fil, et assemble les .ij. chiés ensamble, et estraint l’un a l’autre, et le laisse .i. jor ou .ij.;	and draw the head out with thread, and bring the two heads together, and hold them tightly for one or two days;
et le restraint aucune fois, tant que li filz cope ces chars que sont entre dous, et chiecent;	and restrain it sometimes, as long as the threads draw close to each other, and stick;
puis cure la plaie tant qu’elle soit soudee et sanee.	then cure the wound until it is sealed and healed.
Se li fistule ne perce, si la fai percier en toutes les manieres que tu pues, s’ele n’est trop em parfont.	If the fistula does not drain, then have it drained in every way you can, if it is not too deep.
Car il ne covient mie faire por le lacement coper si em parfont, et puis le cure, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	For it is not advisable to bandage it so tightly during the bleeding, and then during the treatment, as we have said, until he is healed.
Li forme dou spatumile espinous dont on fent la fistule si est mout agus d’une, part et trenchans;	The form of the spiny sputum which they make into a fistula is very sharp on one side and pointed;
et d’autre part non, por ceu c’on ne cope mie ceu c’on ne doit mie copeir, si com tu vois ci:	and on the other side it is not, so that one should not bandage it as one should not bandage, as you see here:
des emorroydes	of hemorrhoids
Emorrydes sont selonc ij. manieres: ou elles sont dedens le fondement, ausi com grain de resin, et s’en i a petites et grans, et en cort adés sanc,	Hemorrhoids are of two types: they can be inside the anus, like grains of resin, and there are small and large ones, and they ooze blood.
et s’en i a une ou plusors, et sont defuer le fondement et au chief dou fondement; mais celles qui sont defuer si ont poc de moistor,	And there can be one or more of them, and some are outside the anus and at the top of the anus; but those that are outside have little moisture.and those inside ooze blood.
et encort adés ou un poc d’aigue citrine ou un poc de sanc, et ont la color dou cors;	And they ooze a little water or a little blood, and they are the color of the body;
et li cure de ces qui les ont dedens le fondement, si est que tu comandes au malaide qu’il s’espreigne por aleir en chambres, tant que li fondemens li isse fuer, et c’aperent li filz;	And the treatment for those who have them inside the anus is that you command the patient to stretch themselves out in bed, until the hemorrhoids emerge and the veins are exposed;
si te haste, et le pent as tenailles, ou tu le tien a ton ungle, puis le cope en ses racines;	If you are in a hurry, seize it with tongs or your fingernail, then pull it out by its roots.
et se li uncine ne les pueent tenir por ses moistors, si les prent a .i. drapeil, ou a couton, ou d’une piece de chamelot;	And if the nails cannot hold it due to moisture, then grab it with a cloth, or cotton, or a piece of camel's hair.
et les estrai a tes dois, puis les cope, et poudre desus aucunes chaudes poudres que soient en leu de cautere;	Pull them out with your fingers, then cut them, and powder some hot powdered medicine on them, which is in place of cauterization.
ou tu les cauterize si com il est dit ou chapistre de cautere, puis les cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez;	Or you can cauterize them as stated in the chapter on cauterization, then treat them with other treatments until they are healed.
et se li fondemens ne puet issir, si clisterize le malaide de clistere mordant et aspre por laver ceu qui est ou fondement, si qu’il puist issir apertement;	and if the fundament cannot emerge, then cleanse the patient with a sharp and rough enema to wash away what is in the fundament so that it may emerge clearly.
cant li malaides se preint, et se li fil sont fuer dou fondement, si est li cure legiere;	when the patient defecates, and if the thread is drawn out from the fundament, then the cure is easy.
et est que tu les preignes a ton ungle ou as tenailles, et les cope, puis les cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez, et qu’il redoute l’incision par fer.	and you should pull them with your fingernail or tweezers, and cut them, then cure them as we have said, until they are healed and fear the incision by iron.
Si covient que tu amenistre la costure selonc ceste maniere: pren .i. fil tort, et le boute en une aguille, et puis trai le fil au desus et fai percier l’aguille d’autre part, et torne les .ij. chiez dou fil desoz l’aguille,	If you must administer the suture according to this method: take a twisted thread and put it in a needle, then pull the thread through the top and pierce the needle from another side, and turn both ends of the thread under the needle,
et si soit dou large; et estraint le fil forment, puis noe le fil, et estrai l’aguille, et fai ensi de toz les autres, et en laisse .i. por corre la superfluiteit dou sanc;	and if it is too wide; then tighten the thread tightly, then tie a knot in the thread, and pull out the needle, and do likewise with all the others, and leave one to draw off the excess blood;
puis met sus le fondement .i. drapeil moilliet en oile roset ou en cerote, et met sus le fondement, et comande au malaide k’il repose;	then place over the wound a damp cloth moistened with rose oil or with cerate, and put it on the wound, and instruct the patient to rest;
et puis le laisse tant qu’il chiecent, et quant il seront cheut, si les cure d’oignement et d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and then let him defecate, and when he has defecated, then cleanse him with ointments and other remedies until he is healed.
dou sechement dou fiens ou fondement	from dryness of the anus or rectum
Maintes fois avient sechement de fiens en l’intestine, et par constrignement de nature, et quant li maladie est vielle et medicine n’i vaut.	Drying of the bowels occurs often in the intestines, due to constipation or when the illness is old and medicine doesn't help.
Si covient que tu reses a la point d’un spatumile ou a ton ungle l’escorce desus, qui ne le laisse a moistir;	You should cut away at the end of a spatula or your fingernail, scraping off the top layer which doesn't allow moisture through.
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sodez si com il covient;	Then dry it until it is completely dry as it ought to be.
et s’il ne puet soder, si rencomence la rasure plus fort que devant, tant qu’il saine mout, et soit escorchiez;	And if it cannot be dried, then scrape away more aggressively than before until it heals and is completely dry.
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	then cure it until it is healed.
dou fremit	where there is trembling
Formice est une petite apparance fautree antor le cors, et va mout em parfont;	A flea is a small creature that creeps under the body and bites deeply;
et aucune fois la trueve li frois, et le sent on ausi comme mort de fremit, et vient en tout le cors, et plus as mains que autre part.	and sometimes it bites, and one feels it like a deathly trembling, and it comes over the whole body, more so in the hands than anywhere else.
Et li cure si est que tu pren une cainne d’une penne d’oie, ou une penne de vultul fort, et met celle caine sus le fremit, tant que li cercles porpreigne le fremit tot entor;	And the treatment is that you take a feather of an goose's feather, or a strong vulture's feather, and put this feather on the vein, so that the purple circle covers the vein all around;
puis torne ta main a tout la cainne tant que tu copes tout entor le fremit, et le met em parfont, et esraiche le fremit de ses racines.	then turn your hand along the whole feather until you feel all around the vein, and push it in deeply, and squeeze the vein from its roots.
Et se tu vues, si fai ceu d’une caine d’arain ou de fer selonc ceste forme, et soit subtilz desoz et traians desus:	And if you see, make this out of a feather of bronze or iron according to this shape, and let it be thin underneath and curved on top.
ne mie perciet, por mues tenir au doi, et mues presser Et se tu vues, si cauterize lou fremit, si com il est devant ou chapistre de cautere.	do not pierce it, so that it can hold the vein, and squeeze it And if you see, cauterize the vein, as it is before in the chapter on cauterization.
de la forme dou clistere	of the form of the enema
Aucune fois fait on clistere d’argent ou d’archaut, ou d’arain fondut ou mailliet; et aucune fois fait on de ces estrumens petis et grans, selonc ces a cui il sont amenistrez.	Sometimes an enema is made of silver or brass, or of melted copper or small and large stones, depending on the person to whom they are administered.
Cil donques c’on amenistre en la cure des enfans et qui sont foible et dolorous, sont petis.	Those which are administered to children and those who are weak and in pain are small.
Li forme dou clistere petit et grant si est desus large, ou li ventres est liiez selonc ceste maniere:	The form of the small and large enema is above wide, or the stomach is bound according to this manner:
et i ait une desevrance ou li ventres soit liiez, si com tu vois, et li chiez soit dedens perciez; et ait a l’un des costez .ij. pertus, et en l’autre .i.;	and it has an opening where the belly is tied, as you see, and the anus is pierced inside; and it has two openings on one side, and one on the other;
et soit li ventres ou om met les medicines d’une vessie de beste ou de parchemin, et soit perciez tout entor de menus pertus,	and the belly where one puts the medicines is made of a beast's bladder or parchment, and it is pierced all around with small holes;
et ait entre chescun pertus .i. doit d’espaice, puis boute en ces pertus .i. fil fort de fil crut tort en .x. ou enqui entor, et assemble le ventre si com est une chievre;	and there is one inch between each hole, then insert one strong thread of twisted yarn into each hole, and gather the belly together like a goat's skin;
et quant li medicine est dedens, si la lie a l’estrument devant d’un fil fort, puis clisterize; et c’est li forme dou cercle:	and when the medicine is inside, tie it to the instrument with a strong thread, then catheterize; and this is the shape of the circle:
Et soit li medicine ne trop chaude ne trop froide, et oint le chief dou clistere d’oile ou d’aubun d’uef, ou de semblant chose, puis le boute ens legierement;	Let the medicine not be too hot nor too cold, and anoint the head of the catheter with oil or egg white, or similar, then insert it gently.
puis l’espreigne li ministres a ses .ij. mains ensamble, tant qu’il soit toz vuis, puis estrai lou clistere, et lieve li malaides ses jambes a la paroit,	Then the operator squeezes the bulb with both hands simultaneously until it is empty, then withdraws the catheter and leaves the patient lying on his back.
et se li medicine vuet issir, si la teigne tant com il puet; et s’il dort une nuit atot, si est plus grans aide.	And if the medicine wants to come out, let him hold it as long as he can; and if he sleeps for a night afterward, it is even better.
Et se tu le clisterizes em maladie de decorrement de ventre, et li medicine se haste d’issir, si le rencomence tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if you catheterize him for a flux of the belly, and the medicine rushes out, then he should repeat it until he is cured.
Et se li emorroide sont ou fondement, ou aposteme, si soit li clistere ausi subtilz com por .i. enfant;	And if the hemorrhoids are in the anus, or an abscess, then the enema should be as thin as for a child.
et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil sus coi li cuir soit estraint:	and this is the form of the thin enema that causes the skin to stretch:
des plaies	wounds
Nos avons jai dit en la division la cure des plaies; or vos dirons les cures de mains et de medicine, selonc l’acomplissement.	We have already discussed in the division about the treatment of wounds; now we will discuss the treatments by hand and medicine, according to the completion.
Je dis que les plaies sont diverses selonc ceu qu’elles sont faites, et selonc les leus ou les plaies sont faites, et de coi elles sont faites.	I say that wounds are diverse according to how they are made, and according to the places where the wounds are made, and according to what makes them.
Les choses par coi plaies sont faites sont par gitement de piere, et taille d’espee et de couteil, ou de lance ou de fust ou de siette, ou de semblans choses;	The things by which wounds are made are by stone, and cutting with a sword or knife, or with a spear, staff, arrow, or similar objects.
ou que sont faites selonc les leus dou cors, si com plaie que chiet sus le col, ou sus le chief, ou le peis, ou le ventre, ou le foie, et semblans membres;	Or they are made according to the places in the body, such as a wound that falls on the neck, head, foot, belly, liver, and similar organs;or it is made by fire, or cold, or both, or by wind, or by moisture, or by dryness, or by change of weather, or by change of place, or by change of food and drink.
et je vos dirai la cure de chescune plaie, et encomencerai as plaies dou chief simples, car li remenbrance venra en son chapistre.	And I will tell you the treatment for each wound, and I will begin with simple head wounds, since the memory will come in its chapter.
Je dis que quant simple plaie vient ou chief, et li os n’est brisiez, si pren garde se c’est de gitement de piere ou de semblans choses, et li cuir est toutevoie rompus et est li plaie grans,	I say that when a simple wound comes to the head and the bone is not broken, one should take care if it is from a blow of stone or similar things, and the skin is still broken and the wound is large,
et tu doutes levement d’aposteme chaut: si le fai tantost sainier de la cephalique meismement s’il vient poc de sanc de la plaie, et soit li sainie au contraire de la partie navree;	and you fear a hot abscess quickly: then make the wound bleed from the cephalic vein immediately if there is little blood coming from the wound, and let the bleeding be in the opposite direction of the injured part;
et eschuisse li malaides repletion de vin et de viandes grosses.	and reduce the patient's consumption of wine and rich foods.
Et s’il ne vuet sainier, si soit amenuisie sa viande, et ne boive point de vin, ne ne menjuce point de char;	And if he does not want to bleed, then his diet should be reduced, and he should not drink wine or eat rich food;
et met sor la plaie, se apostemes chaus i vient, coton moilliet en oile roset soulement, ou en vin stiptice;	and put sore on the wound, if hot abscesses come, moistened cotton in rose oil only, or in astringent wine;
et s’il n’i a aposteme chaut, si met sus la plaie, s’elle est fresche a tout son sanc, et elle n’est muee par l’air, poudre, que je dirai un poc ci aprés;	and if there is no hot abscess, put on the wound, if it is fresh and bleeding, and has not been moved by air, powder that I will describe shortly:
et se li ars l’ait muee, si met sus aucuns oignemens, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and if the wound has been moved by the heat, put on some ointments until it is healed.
Et se li plaie est grans si com de tailleure d’espee et de semblans, et les levres ne se pueent assembler par tentes, si les assemble par cousture, si com je dirai as plaies dou ventre, de la costure.	And if the wound is large like that of a sword and similar, and the lips cannot be brought together with stitches, then bring them together with sutures, as I will describe for abdominal wounds.
Se li plaie est descoverte de l’os, et pent, et ne tient mais que a un poc, si le cope; puis cure la plaie de medicine, et restoure char dure en leu de cuir,	If the wound is exposed to the bone, and it can be reached, and holds only by a little, then cut it off; then cure the wound with medicine, and restore hard flesh in place of skin,
et comande au malaide a mengier grosses viandes, si com testes et froment cuit, ausi com poulz, et semblans choses.	and instruct the patient to eat coarse foods, such as testicles and cooked wheat, also as poultry, and similar things.
Et se tu trueves ou cuir porriture, et il n’aert a l’os, si cope lou porrit tot, et giete fuer, puis le cure;	And if you find pus in the skin, and it is not close to the bone, then cut out the pus completely, and pour it out, then cure it;
et se il ait artere en la plaie ou voine, dont sans cort, et il ne puet estainchier par medicines, si quier l’artere, et se tu la trueves desloie, si la lie d’un fil;	and if there is an artery in the wound or vein, which bleeds profusely and cannot be staunched by medicine, then tie it off with a thread;
et se ceu ne profite mie, si la cauterize.	and if this does not help, then cauterize it.
Et se ces plaies sont petites et simples, si est li cure legiere: et est que tu mettes ens ceste poudre qui soude ainsois que li ars l’ait muee.	And if these wounds are small and simple, the cure is easy: you must apply this powder which will heal as soon as the burn has healed.
Et li maniere de la poudre si est: pren encens une partie; sanc de dragon .ij. parties; chalz vive .iij. parties, et le poudre subtilment,	And the way to make the powder is: take incense one part, dragon's blood two parts, quicklime three parts, and grind them together finely,
et emple la plaie, et l’estraint forment, tant qu’elle s’aerse bien et se joigne a tout son sanc;	and apply it to the wound, and hold it firmly until it is well healed and joined to the flesh;
et puis la lie bien, et la laisse sens desliier, s’elle n’enfle; car on n’oste la madicine tant qu’ele soit sanee.	and then bandage it well, leaving it untied if it is swollen; for the medicine is not removed until it has healed.
Et aucune fois fait on ceu de chalz soulement, quant on n’ait l’encens ne lou sanc de dragon, mais que li ars n’ait muee la plaie.	And sometimes one should use chalks only when one doesn't have incense or dragon's blood, but only when the wound has healed.
Et se li ars ait mueit la plaie, meismement en esteit, si n’i met om mie ceste poudre;	And if the wound is not healed, then one should use this powder:
mais met sus aucuns oignemens digestis, ou poulz de farine d’orge faites d’aigue et de miel, tant qu’ele giete bowe;	but place some digestive ointments or barley flour made with water and honey on the wound until it becomes dry.
puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	then treat other treatments until he is healed.
Et se li brisure d’os vient avec la plaie, et elle est petite, si l’estrai as pinceures subtilz;	And if the fracture of the bone comes with the wound, and it is small, then extract it with subtle pincers;
et je vos dirai ci aprés les brisures dou chief.	and I will tell you about head fractures after.
de la plaie dou col	of the wound in the neck
Se plaie vient ou col et elle est simple, si n’a point de difference entre li et celi dou chief, mais se li ners dou col ou li artere est copee.	If the wound is on the neck and it is single, there is no difference between it and that of the head, except that the nerves or artery of the neck may be cut.
Se c’est li ners, si n’i a autre engien que laissier la cure, et n’i mettre nulle chose restraignant, car il nuit as ners et les fait retraire;	If it is the nerve, there is nothing else to do but let it be and put nothing on it that would constrict, for it hurts the nerves and makes them withdraw.
et ne mettre sus la plaie rien froit, car li substance des ners est froide, et li continuation d’aus si est avec le cerveil, qui est li plus haus membres;	And put nothing cold on the wound, for the substance of the nerves is cold, and their continuation is with the brain, which is the highest member.
mais soit li medicine souez, si com chalz lavee en aigue douce, et mellee avec oile roset, et cucie lavee ausi en aigue douce,	But the medicine should be warm, like chalk washed in sweet water and mixed with rose oil, and cooked washed also in sweet water,
et autres pieres de mine selonc ceste maniere, et oignemens moistes.	and other moist stones according to this manner.
Et se li plaie est grans, si la cout et lie de bendes, puis la cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the wound is large, cut and ligature it with bandages, then treat it until it is healed.
Et se les plaies sont parfondes et ele est chevee et pleinne de bowe, si la perce ou plus bas leu;	And if the wounds are deep and she is pregnant and full of bowels, so pierce her at a lower place;
et se li artere est copee, et decorremens de sanc en vient, si la desoivre, et la loie, et la cauterize se mestier est;	and if the artery is cut, and bleeding comes from it, then ligature it, and let it be, and cauterize it if necessary;
et se li espinee de la gorge est copee, ou li keurs, et li conduiz est gardez, par coi la viande va,	and if the spine of the throat is cut, or the carotid, and the conduit is kept, through which the meat goes,
si cout le keur sus la cainne de la gorge, et ne touchier la gorge mais la remet selonc sa figure naturel;	if it cuts the carotid above the throat, and does not touch the throat but puts it back according to its natural shape;
et puis l’estrain avenanment, et le laisse aucuns jors, puis le cure d’oignemens desechans tant qu’il soit sanez;	and then strains it gently, and leaves it for a few days, then heals it with purifying poultices until it is healed;
et se li plaie a fait empression en l’os, si la quier;	and if the wound has made an impression in the bone, then it wants;
et s’il i a pieces d’os, si les trai fuers toz se tu pues, et ces que tu ne pues avoir, si laisse tant que li plaie porrisse,	and if there are pieces of bone, draw out all that you can, and those that you cannot reach, leave as they are until the wound heals.
et soit desevree et aligie li issue;	and the dislocation should be readjusted and aligned with its proper position.
et se li plaie est fresche, si poudre sus la poudre que j’ai dit.	And if the wound is fresh, put powder on the powder that I have described.
Et s’il a en la plaie os et il i a fistule, si la cure ensi com j’ai dit en son chapistre.	And if there is bone in the wound and there is a fistula, treat it as I have described in its chapter.
de la plaie de lance ou de coutel	of the wound of spear or knife
Se c’est cop de lance ou de coutel, et li plaie est parfonde, si regarde se de la plaie saut ventositez cant li malaides alainne: saiches adonques que li plaie est mortelz;	If it is a spear or knife wound and the wound is deep, then look to see if from the wound wind escapes: know therefore that the wound is deadly;
et s’elle n’est parfonde, et elle est fresche a tout son sanc, si n’i mettre mie a la premiere houre la poudre, ne ne la liier mie por le sanc que ne demorse em parfont,	and if it is not deep but the wound is fresh and bleeding profusely, then do not put on the powder at first, nor ligature it for the blood that escapes profusely,
et reviegne au cuer, et ocie lou malaide;	and let the patient rest;
mais i met oignement atractif, et le lie .ij. fois le jor;	but I apply an attractive ointment, and bind it .ii. times a day;
et se tu n’as oignement, si met en la plaie viel coton por succier fuers la moistor,	and if you do not have ointment, put old cotton in the wound to draw out moisture,
et fai dormir le malaide sus la plaie .iij. jors, ou .iiij., ou plusors;	and let the patient sleep on the wound for 3, or 4, or more days;
si n’i venra mie spasme, ne tremor male de cuer n’es traingnemens d’alainne;	if there comes no cramp, nor trembling of the heart, nor twitching of the eyes;
et quant tu vois les bones dispositions, si saiches que li plaie est sauve.	and when you see good healing, then you know that the wound is saved.
Cure la donques de tentes et d’autres cures, tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then treat it with poultices and other remedies until it is healed;
et s’elle ne puet saner, et oevre, adés saiches que il i a fistule; si la cure si com on doit.	and if it cannot heal, and there is an abscess, then you know that there is a fistula; so treat it as it should be treated.
Et se li plaie est d’incision d’espee ou de coutel, et elle est simple, ou pis ou au dos, si la cure de ceu qui est devant;	And if the wound is from a sword or knife, and it is simple, or worse, on the back, then treat it as one who is in front;
s’elle est grans, de cousture; et s’elle est petite, de poudre, et s’elle est empressee en l’os, et en a copeit pieces, si quier la plaie, et les trai fuers s’il sont desevrez;	if it is large, with stitching; and if it is small, with powder, and if it is pressed into the bone, and has torn fragments, then treat the wound, and pull out the foreign objects if they are loose.
et s’il ne sont desevrez, si laisse porrir la plaie, si aligera li estractions;	and if they are not loose, let the wound fester so that the extractions can be relieved.
et des autres plaies as autres membres est li jugemens si com nos avons dit.	and for other wounds in other limbs, the judgement is as we have said.
dou derrompement dou ventre	from a rupture in the belly
Li derompemens dou ventre est grans et moiens et petis;	There are great, medium, and small ruptures of the belly;
de la grant plaie saut aucune fois li intestine, ou li ners des intestines, par coi li intromission d’aus;	from the large wound sometimes the intestine, or the nerves of the intestines, by which the intestines are introduced;
et li costure est plus malaisie, et aucune fois vaut pis li petite plaie que li grans,	and the sewing is more difficult, and sometimes the smaller wound is worse than the larger one;
por ceu c’on remet plus a poinnes les intestines en, s’on ne les i remet de chaut en chaut;	because one puts them back in more easily when they are warm, if they have become cold;
por ce que li intestine enflent tantost qu’il sentent le froit, si rentrent plus a poinnes,	because the intestines swell as soon as they feel cold, they contract more on their own,
et por ceu vaut mues li moieinne plaie, por ceu c’on ramoine mues l’intestine a son leu que as autres .ij.	and therefore it is better for the smaller wound to reset the intestine to its place rather than the others. 2
Et saiches que li routure dou ventre est selonc .iiij. manieres:	And you should know that there are four types of hernia in the belly:
les .ij. costures communes avienent en la costure dou ventre,	The first two common ones occur in the abdominal wall,
et li costure des autres plaies dou cors et .ij. autres costures propres sont communes as autres plaies;	and the suturing of other wounds on the body, and another two proper sutures are common to other wounds;
et toutevoie elles sont plus propres avec la costure dou ventre, et je dirai une chescune et declairerai.	and nonetheless they are more suitable with the suturing of the abdomen, and I will describe each one and explain.
Je di que quant li plaie est petite, et aucune chose de l’intestine ist fuer,	I say that when the wound is small, and no intestine protrudes,
et griés chose est dou remettre, ceu est par l’une des .ij. manieres:	and little needs to be done, this is by one of two methods:
ou por la petitece de la plaie, si com nos avons dit,	or by the smallness of the wound, as we have said,
ou por ce que li intestine est enflez por le froit.	or because the intestines are swollen from the cold.
Et quant il est frois, eschaufez lou en teil maniere:	And when it is cold, warm it in such a way:
moillie une esponge ou .i. mol drapeil en aigue tede soulement,	wet a sponge or soft cloth with lukewarm water,
ou tu cuis en aigue squinant et cipre et spique,	or you cook in hot water with squinant, cypress, and spike.
et arose l’intestine tant que li enfleure soit ostee;	and you wash the intestines until they are clean;
et aucune fois fait ce vins restraingnans, et est muedre que awe soule por desenfler.	and sometimes this wine is made constricting, and it is better to drink it to reduce swelling.
Et quant tu vois l’enfleure departir, si amoiste l’intestine d’aigue ou altee et malves soient cuites,	And when you see the swelling go down, then cook the intestines in water or altus and malvasia,
car par ceu est aligie li entree a poc de chose;	for by this the entrance is blocked with very little.
et s’il n’i puet entrer, si fent un poc la plaie a l’estrument de coi on cope les emorroydes;	and if it cannot enter, then they make a small wound with the instrument used to cut out hemorrhoids;
et li premiere cure est muedre que li taille,	and the first treatment is bloodletting rather than cutting,
que nus n’i doit taillier sens grant necessiteit n’i ait;	which one should not cut without great need;
et c’est li estrumens por le fendre:	and this is the tool to split it with:
si trenche dedens en la corbeure et defuer non, et vez ci la forme:	it cuts within the curve and out, and see here the shape:
Et quant li plaie est enlargie, et li intestine saut fuer,	And when the wound is enlarged and the intestines jump out,
si le remet arer selonc la forme naturel en son leu propre,	if he puts it back according to its natural shape in its proper place,
se tu en as pooir, car ce vaut mues.	if you have the power, for this is worth it.
Quant li plaie est large, et elle est en la partie desoz lou ventre,	When the wound is large, and it is in the lower part of the abdomen,
si covient que tu faices gesir lou malaide sus son dos,	you should make the patient lie on his back,
et met ses jambes plus haut que son chief;	and put his legs above his head;
et s’elle est en la partie desoz le ventre,	and if it is in the part below the belly,
si met le chief et le pis plus haut que les parties desoz,	place the head and feet higher than the parts below.
et ausi se li routure dou ventre est en l’une des .ij. parties	and if the rupture of the belly is in one of the .ii. parts,
si met t’entente en ceu que li partie navree soit plus haute que li autre;	place it so that the wounded part is higher than the other;
et ensi covient amenistrer ceu que je dis en plaies grans et moienes.	and so one should manage what I say about large and small wounds.
Es plaies petites met ceu que t’est apparilliet,	For small wounds, apply what you are experienced with,
puis aies entre tes mains .i. ministre pitous ki teigne toute la routure a sa main,	then have at hand a minister who can stop the bleeding with his hand,
et assemble les levres;	and gather the lips;
et c’est la maniere commune de costures,	and this is the common way of sewing
et est que tu preignes une aguille ou plusors, selonc la quantiteit de la largesce de la plaie,	and you should thread a needle or more, depending on the width of the wound,
puis laisse des le chief de la plaie .i. doi d’espaice, et i fiche une aguille ou il ait .i. boin fil fort;	then leave about a thumb's width from the edge of the wound, and insert a needle with a strong thread through it;
et perce les .ij. chiés dou cuir avec les .ij. chiés dou siphac,	and pierce the two edges of the skin with the two edges of the wound,
qui est desoz le cuir dedens, tant que tu la faices percier de celle partie,	which is underneath the skin, so that you make it pierce from that part,
et assemble les .ij. chief dou siphac les .iiij. ensamble;	and bring together the two halves of the skull, and put together the four pieces;
puis l’estrain d’un fil double entor l’aguille de .ij. pars,	then pull them tightly with a double thread around the needle in two parts,
puis assemble les .ij. chiés de la plaie avenanment,	then assemble the two halves of the wound smoothly,The following text is a medieval medical treatise written in Old French, around the 12th-13th centuries.
et puis laisse .i. doi d’espaice, et i fiche une autre aguille;	and then leave .I. space, and he pushes another needle;
puis la lie dou fil si com tu as fait la premiere aguille,	then pull the thread through as you did with the first needle,
et ne cesser de ceu faire selonc ceu que tu as mestier des aguilles,	and do not stop doing this according to what you need of the needles,
tant que toute li plaie soit restrainte;	until all the wound is closed;
et soient les aguilles moienes, entre subtilz et grosses,	let the needles be medium-sized, between fine and thick,
car les aguilles subtilz copent toute la char, et les trop grosses si ne pueent mie bien entrer:	because fine needles pierce all the flesh, and very thick ones cannot enter well enough:
por ceu covient qu’elles soient moienes;	therefore they should be medium-sized;
et ne covient mie bouter les aguilles trop au defuer de la char et dou cuir,	and one must not push the needles too deep into the flesh and through the skin,
k’elles ne copent et oevrent la plaie devant la soudure;	that they do not cut and open the wound before healing.
et puis cope les chiés des aguilles, qu’elles ne blecent lou malaide au dormir,	and then cut the tips of the needles so that they do not poke the patient while sleeping,
et i met tentes ou drapelz au chiés des aguilles por mues tenir,	and put tents or sheets on the tips of the needles to keep them from moving,
et les laisse tant que li plaie soit soudee;	and leave them until the wound is healed;
et ceste maniere de costure as aguilles est plus covenauble en petites plaies,	and this method of sewing with needles is more suitable for small wounds,
car il i soffist une aguille ou .ij.	because it requires only one needle or two.
Li seconde costure si est commune,	The second stitch is common,
et est que tu assemble les .ij. chiés dou cuir et les .ij. chiés dou syfac ensamble a une aguille ou il ait .i. fort fil moien;	and it is that you join the two edges of the skin and the two edges of the wound together with one needle and a strong, thin thread;
